Memel: Voting Time Extended; Minor Conflicts on the German Border Result in Five Injuries; Hitler Arrives in East Prussia for the First Time 49

The election for the Memel Parliament was originally scheduled to end yesterday, but due to different voting arrangements, it was necessary to extend the voting from 8:00 AM this morning until 6:00 PM tonight. There were minor conflicts yesterday. In a village on the German border, not far from Memel, Germans and Lithuanians engaged in a brawl, resulting in five injuries. Yesterday at 6:00 PM, the original closing time for voting, seventy-six polling places were still surrounded by voters waiting to vote. Fortunately, the cabinet held an emergency meeting and quickly issued a notice extending the voting time. It was later decided that the polling places would remain open today, thus preventing serious disputes from erupting. Yesterday, some people waited for seven hours without being able to vote. Most Germans ridiculed this farcical situation. German and Lithuanian personnel managing the polling places had some unimportant quarrels yesterday. (20th Reuters Telegram)

Memel: The Lithuanian Cabinet today revised the election law, so Memel will continue the election from 8:00 AM to 6:00 PM tomorrow. Because voting is very slow, no more than eighty voters can pass through a polling station per hour. Therefore, in electoral districts with more than one thousand voters, it is impossible to complete voting within the twelve hours stipulated by the election law. Voting began at 8:00 AM this morning, but at 7:00 AM, voters were already lined up in front of the polling stations. The majority of people in the streets are Lithuanian, and order is maintained by Lithuanians, not the Memel police. It is reported that Lithuanian police, at the request of the Memel Electoral Commission, entered the Memel City Government last night. The Memel ballots are now entirely in the hands of the Lithuanian police. (29th National Telegram)

Memel: The voting results will not be announced until tomorrow evening. The reason for extending the voting time is that German voters deliberately obstructed the voting, causing the voting to proceed slowly. Most German voters first gathered at the entrance of the polling station and took half an hour to enter the polling station. Then, they lined up at the entrance of the polling station and entered in an orderly manner. At some polling stations, up to five hundred people were waiting in line. Many Lithuanian farmers returned home after waiting for four hours without being able to vote. Therefore, the authorities initially announced that the voting would be extended until nighttime and then decided to continue voting tomorrow. Today, diplomatic representatives from the United Kingdom, France, and Italy, who guarantee the autonomy of Memel, were present to observe. (29th Havas Telegram)

(Berlin) At the time of the reorganization of the Memel Autonomous Parliament, Führer Hitler took a train to East Prussia last night in a state of embarrassment. Political figures were surprised to hear this news, because since taking office, the Führer has crossed the Polish Corridor to go to East Prussia, this is still the first time. Some people interpret the Führer's visit as a sign of opposition to Lithuania. The general public also expects the Führer to deliver a speech to the Germanic people in the Memel region tomorrow. It is also heard that according to the planned itinerary, Hitler will go to Tannenberg in East Prussia on October 2nd to attend the reburial ceremony of the late President Hindenburg, who passed away last year. After his death, he was buried under the general's tower in that place. The reburial will take place on that day in the final determined tomb. (30th Havas Telegram)

Warsaw: Polish newspapers believe that the new election system in Memel has many shortcomings, providing future Germans with excuses for various disturbances. German Propaganda Minister Delivers Speech on Domestic and Foreign Affairs at Military-Civilian Joint Celebration 50

Karlsruhe, Germany: A joint military-civilian celebration was held here recently. Propaganda Minister Goebbels attended and delivered a speech, elaborating on various domestic and foreign issues in Germany. First, regarding the Jewish question, he said that it should be resolved by the state. The House of Representatives had already passed a law on determining the status of Jews at a meeting in Nuremberg on the 15th of this month. Once the government issues implementing regulations based on this law, any Jew who still cannot behave and abide by the law is an enemy of the state and should be punished by the state. As for the church dispute, the current world situation is so tense that the state must have complete control over the strength of the entire country. This is not only true in terms of military organization, but also in preserving moral resistance. Therefore, no riots should occur among the German people due to religious disputes. In short, the church can preach peacefully in the church, and we should preach to the people on the podium. Although we do not interfere with each other, we must jointly preserve the political unity of the country and not allow it to be damaged in the slightest." Goebbels then mentioned the Memel region, saying, "If there are no law-abiding people in the world, there is no need to talk about the law. Germany's withdrawal from the League of Nations was based on this view, because the League of Nations treats National Socialist Germany in the same way it treated the Weimar Republic after the Great War. Since the League of Nations despises the legitimate demands of the new Germany, Germany disdains to interact with it." (30th Havas Telegram)

US Budget Balanced; White House Issues Announcement; Economic Situation Greatly Improved; No Need to Increase New Taxes 51

(Washington) The White House today, during President Roosevelt's tour, released a revised budget for the federal government for 1937, intending to balance the government's revenue and expenditure without increasing taxes. The White House also issued a presidential announcement, which did not explicitly state the timing of the budget balance, but stated that it could not be achieved before 1938 at the earliest. The total expenditure in the revised budget is $7,752,332,000, while the original budget was $8,520,413,609. The total revenue in the revised budget is $4,470,349,140, while the original budget was $3,991,904,639. The difference between revenue and expenditure is $3,281,982,860 in the new budget, while the original budget was $4,528,508,970. The President also said that the government's tax base is now more solid than before, because ordinary commercial income can generate considerable tax revenue to meet all necessary purposes. The gap between revenue and expenditure in next year's budget has been greatly reduced, so the government will not need to implement new taxes or increase existing tax rates. A spokesperson on the side believes that the government's revised budget this time is the first step towards balancing the budget. (29th National News Agency Telegram)

(Washington) President Roosevelt today made optimistic remarks about the US budget for the 1935-1936 fiscal year, saying that the budget figures indicate that the economic situation is better than in the past three years. He also said that current industrial production and trade are still expanding, and it is expected that the shortfall in 1936-1937 can be reduced compared to the past, and there is no need to greatly increase taxes. As for the shortfall in 1935-1936, it was purely due to temporary expenditures, and most of this expenditure was used for unemployment relief. The 1937 budget is currently being prepared, and efforts are being made to reduce the distance between revenue and expenditure, so the government can avoid proposing new methods to make up for necessary expenses and recover public debt under the current tax plan. President Roosevelt estimated that the shortfall in 1935-1936 would be about 300 million yuan lower than in 1924-1935. Various handling fees will continue to be collected, but if the court accepts lawsuits against this plan, it will encounter the difficulty of finding other ways to collect taxes to meet special expenses. The total shortfall for 1935-1936 is about $3,281,000,000. Excluding the recovery of national debt, the net shortfall is $2,731,000,000. The progress of the work relief program is indeed slower than he hoped, but it is being accelerated. In the coming months, it should be able to provide sufficient work for the unemployed. The estimated revenue for 1925-1936 is $4,470,000,000, and the expenditure is $7,752,000,000. It is also estimated that the total public debt on June 20, 1936, will be $30,723,000,000, which is $2,023,000,000 less than the total public debt on June 30, 1926. Local people believe that President Roosevelt's statement that he does not intend to propose new taxes at present means that President Roosevelt does intend to give the industry some breathing room. (29th Reuters Telegram)

President Roosevelt's Western Tour Arrives in Salt Lake City; Welcomed by Crowds Along the Way 52

Los Angeles: President Roosevelt and his entourage set off for the West Coast today. During the President's tour, whenever the train stopped briefly, a large number of people gathered at the station and cheered loudly, wanting to see Roosevelt's appearance. Therefore, the people traveling with him were very happy, believing that this point can indicate that the extent to which Roosevelt is loved in the agricultural areas of the Midwestern United States has not diminished in the slightest. (29th National Telegram)

War Atmosphere Permeates Europe; Cash Concentrated in the United States; Accounts for 43% of the World; Silver Reserves in the UK and Italy Insufficient for Wartime Use 53

(Washington) According to experts here, if a major war breaks out in Europe, the use of silver, nickel, and other metals in European countries will greatly increase, because cash is concentrated in the United States, and it is already in short supply elsewhere. According to the latest announcement from the US Federal Reserve, the United States currently holds as much as 9.23 billion yuan in cash. Currently, there is still 16.3 million yuan in cash en route to the United States. In summary, of the world's monetary gold, which is about 21.6 billion yuan, the United States holds 43%, France currently has 22%, and the rest is divided among the countries of the world. If the UK and Italy participate in the war in the future, they will certainly not be able to borrow from the United States again. Therefore, experts believe that these countries may use other metals as substitutes or issue more banknotes, implementing inflation. As for the amount of silver reserves in the UK, according to the latest unofficial estimate, it is worth about 70 million pounds. The silver reserves in Italy are worth about 50 million US dollars. Although most of these silver reserves can be minted into subsidiary coins, they will not be sufficient for wartime use. Therefore, paper money or other substitute metals may be used at that time. (29th National Telegram)

Japan National Census 54

(Tokyo) The fourth national census will be conducted simultaneously across the country at 0:00 AM tomorrow. The Tokyo City Government established a temporary national census department on the 4th and will dispatch 13,000 investigators after September 21st to ensure the completeness of the investigation. The items that each household head should record include five items: name, gender, marital status, date of birth, and permanent residence. However, Tokyo City will additionally investigate the date of residence in Tokyo, place of birth, and nationality. In addition, vagrants will be strictly investigated in each district from tonight until 4:00 AM tomorrow. Those living on the water will be investigated by 200 members of the Water Police Department. (30th Dentsu Telegram)

(Tokyo) Japan's fourth national census will be implemented uniformly across the country and overseas tonight at midnight, or 0:00 AM on October 1st. The reporting forms have been sent to all Japanese people around the world. According to the results of the third national census in Showa 5 (1930), Japan's population was 90,396,043, an increase of 6,939,114 compared to the second census. It is expected that the result of this census will be approximately 99 million people. (30th Nihon Rengo Telegram)

Frankfurt, Germany: Dr. Yan Huiqing, Chinese Ambassador to Russia and representative to the League of Nations, has been lingering here for two days. (30th Central News Agency Telegram)

Revised Examination Regulations Promulgated 59

(Nanjing) The Examination Yuan has promulgated and implemented a total of twelve revised examination regulations. Slight changes have been made to the general examination methods in border areas. The new regulations stipulate that passing the examination requires a score of 60 or more in each subject of the examination. However, the general examination is divided into two types, A and B. Type A requires a score of 60 or more in each subject, while Type B requires an average score of 60 or more. However, the passing method for Type B of the general examination is limited to remote provinces where the number of people receiving education is relatively small. (30th Central News Agency Telegram)

International Commercial Telegraph

—September 30th Reuters Special Commercial Telegram— Gold and Silver

British Gold: The London gold price today was 141 shillings and 6.5 pence, up half a penny.

British Silver: The London silver market price today was unchanged. Spot and futures prices remained at 29 and 3125 pence. The United States bought, speculators sold, and the closing market was stable.

Exchange Rates

British-American: The London foreign exchange market was sluggish today. The opening price of the British-American exchange rate was 4 yuan, 9 jiao, 1 fen, and 5625, up 0625. After the first hour, it fell to 4 yuan, 9 jiao, 1 fen, and 1875, and then remained unchanged.

British-French: The opening price fell by 5 pounds and became 74 francs and 57. At 11:00, it continued to fall by 3 pounds, and then remained unchanged.

Cotton and Wheat

American Cotton: Although the Liverpool cotton price rose, the local cotton market only rose by 1 pound, but the sentiment was good and the demand from the industry was strong. The market price rose by 3 or 4 pounds and then became silent.

American Wheat: The Chicago wheat market opened firmly this morning, 1 pound higher than the closing price on Saturday, because the Liverpool wheat price suddenly rose. The latest price continued to rise by 1 pound and 25 compared to the opening price. Miscellaneous grains did not rise with the wheat market. The opening price was half a pound lower, and then the price continued to fall due to selling.

British Wheat: The Liverpool wheat market lacked sellers this morning, causing the price to rise sharply at 1:00 PM. The October futures price rose by 875 to 6 shillings, 7 pence, and 625.

British Cotton: The Liverpool cotton market turned stable today. At 1:00 PM, the October futures price was 5.87, up 2 pounds.

Rubber

London: The rubber market gradually rose this morning. The opening transaction price for January-March futures was 5 pence and 9375, up 0625 compared to the closing price on Saturday. The noon price was 6 pence.

New York: The London rubber market was extremely stable, so the New York rubber market opened well. The price was 6 pounds higher, and then it continued to rise by 7 pounds because of good demand.

Securities

New York: The stock market opened firmly this morning. Power plant stocks were 625 higher than the closing price on Saturday, but mining stocks fell slightly. Macy's department store stocks also fell by 875, and then recovered by 25. The market trend turned slightly weak during power generation. The average price of Dow Jones' thirty industrial stocks opened at 131.79, up 4 pounds.

Ministry of Finance Urges Preparation of Budgets and Final Accounts 75

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Finance stated that the 23rd year has ended, and a total of three notices have been issued to urge the preparation of the first-level final accounts for that year. Internal agencies in Nanjing should submit them to the ministry before October 31st. External agencies in Nanjing should mail them early to avoid exceeding the deadline. Any further delays will be investigated and punished accordingly. As for the budget for the 25th year, all ministry agencies are now notified that they must submit it to the ministry three months before the beginning of the year and must not exceed the deadline in the slightest. Qin-Yu Area: Smuggling Ring Discovered; Specializing in Transporting Tax-Evading Smuggled Goods for Sale Inside the Pass; Customs Enforcement Resists with Force 91

Tianjin Communication: Within Dongluocheng in Yuguan, there is recently an organization called Xiehe Trading House, managed by Japanese and puppet personnel. Outwardly, it is a transshipment agency, but in reality, it specializes in smuggling operations. What is transported out of the pass are silver bullion, silver coins, and banknotes from the Central Bank and Bank of Communications. What is transported into the pass are goods like ramie yarn, sugar, and rayon. Rumors circulate that a smuggling kingdom has recently emerged between Qin and Yu, and this place serves as its headquarters. In the smuggling ring, people of all nationalities are involved. Each smuggling run consists of three to five or seven to eight people, equipped with weapons. When customs enforcement personnel discover them, they immediately resist with force, almost equivalent to the bandits of a few years ago. In late last month, Qin Island customs personnel seized a large quantity of smuggled rayon. Six or seven customs officers were brutally beaten nearly to death by dozens of ruffians. This is proof of this. Customs anti-smuggling patrol boats, while patrolling at sea, are repeatedly attacked by smuggling vessels. Therefore, since March of this year, the Qin Island customs patrol boats Beijiang and Yulin (each weighing fifty tons) have been equipped with weapons to defend themselves in cases of emergency. Unexpectedly, on September 18, when the two ships sailed back to the Qin Island pier from the Yantai sea area, they were suddenly subjected to the local Japanese military police forcibly confiscating their weapons. One machine gun and ten rifles on each ship were taken away. Customs Commissioner Hao Gede protested to the military police captain Takimoto, which resulted in the release of the ships. However, the Yulin's engine was damaged at some unknown time, and was only repaired and left the port on the 25th. According to the Japanese side, within the war zone, except for the security forces who are allowed to carry arms, other groups and agencies are not allowed to be armed. The customs patrol boats having weapons seems to conflict with the war zone agreement, so they must be confiscated. While this may sound reasonable, in reality, it only weakens the customs patrol force, allowing smuggling vessels to come and go without hindrance in the future. Qin Island Naval Customs Commissioner Hao Gede came to Tianjin on the 27th to meet with Tianjin Customs Superintendent Han Linsheng and Customs Commissioner Baus, to discuss future smuggling prevention measures. It has been decided that all card patrol personnel within the jurisdiction of Qinhuangdao Customs will be rotated with Tianjin Customs employees every six months to prevent smugglers from becoming familiar with their faces and taking unfavorable actions.

A pro-Japanese merchant shop in a certain Tianjin concession is entrusted by smuggling rings to sell their tax-evading goods on one hand, and to collect silver bullion on the other, which is then carried to Shanhaiguan by Korean ruffians. Although the exact amount cannot be determined, the frequency of Korean travelers heading east every day suggests that a considerable amount is being transported. On the 27th of this month, a tragic incident occurred due to smuggling. At 9:15 AM on that day, the Pingyu express train No. 41, traveling from Tianjin to the east, was moving slowly as it departed from the East Station. A Korean man, about thirty years old, carrying a suitcase, frantically ran to catch the train. However, because the suitcase was too heavy and he couldn't run fast enough, one foot had already stepped onto the train steps, but his grip wasn't secure, and he slipped and fell onto the tracks, where he was crushed to death. The scene was gruesome. After the incident, it was found that the suitcase contained 900 silver coins, covered with clothing. The body was taken away by the Korean Residents Association of Tianjin. Because he died due to his own carelessness, no further statement was made. (28th)

Anti-Chinese Sentiment in Siam Intensifies; Heavy Military Taxes Levied on Chinese-Owned Rice Mills; Forced Employment of Siamese Workers; Overseas Chinese Students Prohibited from Wearing Chinese Clothing 92

Guangzhou Communication: Anti-Chinese sentiment in Siam has intensified recently. Initially, overseas Chinese schools were targeted, with mandatory teaching of Siamese in local Chinese schools. Then, local Chinese schools were closed down, and Chinese teachers were expelled from the country. Our country's negotiations with them have been ineffective. The Siamese government, believing they have the upper hand, takes things further. Recently, they have started targeting the commercial and industrial sectors, ostracizing overseas Chinese. They are imposing heavy taxes on rice mills and restricting the employment of Chinese workers, aiming to suffocate their businesses and drive them to ruin, in order to achieve their annexation plan. Returned overseas Chinese from here have established an "Aid Siam Association" to assist the overseas Chinese there and to petition the government to immediately negotiate seriously with the Siamese government to relieve the plight of the overseas Chinese there. The Aid Siam Association yesterday again received two telegrams from overseas Chinese groups in Siam, reporting on the situation of the Siamese government oppressing Chinese workers, which is infuriating. The two telegrams are appended below: (1) "To the Overseas Chinese Associations Committee for Assisting Fellow Overseas Chinese in Siam, Guangzhou: The Siamese government has absolutely no sincerity in revising the harsh anti-Chinese regulations. The slowness of our government's negotiations and the decline of the national spirit have further provoked their brutal intentions. In mid-September, they promulgated extremely severe harsh regulations: 1. Chinese-owned rice mills must allocate half of their annual profits to the Siamese Navy and Air Force. 2. Overseas Chinese in Siam must not engage in any acts that insult the Japanese. 3. Overseas Chinese students are not allowed to wear Chinese clothing. 4. Siamese workers must account for seven-tenths of all workers in Chinese-owned rice mills throughout Siam. Our overseas Chinese are now planning countermeasures day and night. In addition to continuing to send telegrams to our government requesting negotiations, there will be a joint petition during the day. Otherwise, all overseas Chinese will go on strike to achieve success. We deeply hope that your association will provide concrete assistance and awaken the Chinese people to support us unanimously. The overseas Chinese in Siam are extremely fortunate, and the country and the nation are extremely fortunate. We anxiously await your orders, the United Association of Overseas Chinese in Siam, respectful salute, Yang Yin." (2) Telegram from the Rice Mill Workers' Union of Overseas Chinese in Siam: "(Omitted heading) The Siamese government's expulsion of overseas Chinese is becoming increasingly severe. Past actions have not ceased, and new ones are even more intense. It has been found that in mid-September, a new and extremely severe oppression was imposed, requiring all Chinese-owned rice mills in Siam to replace seven-tenths of their workers with Siamese workers, and to allocate half of their annual profits to the Siamese Navy and Air Force. We and others are facing unprecedented pressure and are determined to resist to the death. Otherwise, the disaster will be even greater. Therefore, we have jointly organized a petition delegation with the overseas Chinese rice mills in Siam to negotiate forcefully in order to abolish this. We deeply hope that the officials of the authorities will sympathize with the plight of the overseas Chinese and make serious representations to the Siamese government, and awaken the Chinese people to unite and assist us. We look to the sea and sky, crying out in agony. We eagerly await your urgent response, the Rice Mill Workers' Union of Overseas Chinese in Siam, respectful salute, Geng Yin." (September 24th evening)

The Tragic State of the Yellow River Flood in Pi County: 90% of the Entire County Submerged; Water Conservancy Agencies Neglect Prevention 93

Pi County Communication: Pi County is located in the northern border of Jiangsu Province, with a low-lying terrain and crisscrossing rivers. The summer floods from southern Shandong all use Pi County as their final outlet. Disasters occur nine out of ten years. The residents are impoverished, making it the poorest county in Jiangsu Province. This summer, the Yellow River flooded, flowing from western Shandong into Zhaoyang and Weishan Lakes, and then directly into Pi County through the Grand Canal and the Bulao River. Therefore, the flood disaster in this area is more severe than in any other county. It was found that from the beginning of August this year, the Grand Canal and the Bulao River simultaneously started to rise, but it was very gradual, and the people did not pay attention. The county government, following provincial orders, focused all its efforts on repairing the south bank of the Bulao River, and tacitly abandoned other dikes. By late August, when the main flood arrived, the people spontaneously started repairing the dikes on both sides of the Grand Canal. All the people in the county, all the able-bodied men, and County Magistrate Qin Jieren led personnel from various agencies to supervise the work day and night, without rest. However, due to the vastness of the project and the lack of manpower, coupled with strong winds and heavy rain, the waves rose rapidly. The banks of the Bulao River and the Grand Canal gradually collapsed, and 90% of the entire county was submerged. The new school buildings of the Provincial Grand Canal Rural Normal School mostly collapsed. Countless houses in various villages were toppled. The late autumn crops, mostly ripe, were all submerged because the people were busy day and night preventing the Yellow River flood and had no time to harvest. This is especially regrettable. In addition, this spring, hailstorms caused damage, and most of the winter wheat was destroyed. In some areas south of Pi County, not a single grain was harvested. The autumn harvest, on which they depended for their livelihood, was also lost. The 600,000 people of Pi County truly have nowhere to die. Moreover, the floodwater is several feet deep on the plains, and there is no way to escape. Whenever there is a strong wind, the waves rise, and houses collapse. The sounds of disaster echo through the land, too horrible to bear. Dozens of people drown themselves every day. If the government does not provide relief soon or resettle the people to cultivate new lands, the old and weak will inevitably perish in the bellies of fish, and the young and strong will inevitably resort to desperate measures. This is what the government should pay particular attention to. However, since the founding of the Republic of China, Pi County has paid over 10,000 yuan in levies for Grand Canal management every year, but the Jiangsu Grand Canal Engineering Bureau has never moved an inch of soil for the people of Pi in peacetime, nor has it taken a single cent from the people of Pi in times of crisis. The expenses for flood prevention in Pi are all self-funded, so as not to add disaster upon disaster. If the Grand Canal had been dredged slightly beforehand, and if the Huai River Conservancy Commission had not built dams at the lower reaches to confine the water, the flood situation in Pi County would not have been so severe. Although this disaster was due to natural causes, human factors also played a significant role. The people of Pi truly cannot help but feel resentment.

Jiangxi-Hunan Border: Large-Scale Suppression of Remnant Bandits; Pingxiang, Yichun, Pingjiang, and Liuyang Resume Blockade 94

Nanchang Communication: Currently, only two relatively rampant groups of remnant bandits remain in Jiangxi. One is the remnants of Fang Zhimin's bandits, who are roaming the borders of Jiangxi, Zhejiang, and Anhui, and are being encircled and suppressed by Wei Lihuang, who is leading the armies of three provinces. The other is the remnants of Gao Yongsheng, Zhang Tao, and Xu Yangang, who are appearing in the mountainous areas bordering Pingjiang, Liuyang, Yichun, Pingxiang, Tonggu, Xiushui, and Yangxin. They are being encircled and suppressed by Chen Jicheng, who is leading the forces of the Jiangxi-Hubei-Hunan border area. Except for the Tonggu area, which is still a blockade zone, the remote mountainous areas of Cihua, Huayuan, and Lishi in Yichun and Pingxiang have also seen the influx of Red Bandits, who are smuggling supplies. Commander Tan Daoyuan of the area believes that cutting off the bandits' supplies is extremely important during this large-scale suppression. He therefore obtained approval from the Pacification Commissioner's Office to resume the blockade of the bandit areas bordering Yichun, Pingxiang, Pingjiang, and Liuyang, ensuring that no oil, salt, cloth, medicine, hardware, or any daily necessities can flow into the hands of the bandits to cut off their supplies. As for Kong Hechong, the Commander of the Border Pacification of the three provinces, he is recruiting surrendered scattered bandits and rewarding self-reform in the Xiang-E-Gan border area. The number of surrenders is increasing daily, and the number of bandit weapons seized is also increasing.

Anhui Salt Taxation Divided into Zones; Yangzhou Petition Representatives Return to Beijing to Negotiate 95

Wuhu Communication: Chen Jiqian, the Chief of the Anhui Salt Affairs Inspection Office, following the orders of the Salt Affairs Administration of the Ministry of Finance, revised the method of paying salt taxes on the Anhui side. After this news spread, salt merchants gathered to discuss that this revision would greatly hinder the transportation and sale of Huai salt. In the past, it was convenient for all salt merchants on the shore to distribute the goods according to the number of tickets. However, if the new regulation is changed once, it will be unfavorable for the transportation and sales. Therefore, more than 20 representatives from salt merchants in Yangzhou came to Yan several days ago and petitioned the Anhui Salt Affairs Inspection Office for several days. Regarding the tax payment procedures, they requested that they still be handled according to the previous regulations, in order to ease the merchants' difficulties. Chief Chen Jiqian said that the amendment was carried out by order, and was of a trial nature. The request of the salt merchants could not be accepted immediately. However, if there are difficulties in taxation in the future, he will report it for review and instructions. It is heard that the office has now decided on a method of collecting taxes in a centralized manner, dividing the province into five major zones. Wuhu is the first zone, Datong is the second zone, Yuncao is the third zone, Hefei is the fourth zone, and Shelaiquan is the fifth zone. Wuhu Zone will be the first to be tried, and if it is effective, it will be extended to other zones. This method will be implemented at a meeting of all salt merchants after it is submitted to the Salt Affairs Administration of the Ministry of Finance for approval. It is heard that some salt merchants have tacitly acknowledged this, while another group left Wuhu for Beijing today (29th) to conduct further negotiations with the Salt Affairs Administration. Current Status of Luotong Highway Construction in Henan Province: Most of the Luoning and Wen Pass Sections Completed; Ninglu and Luwen Sections Under Construction 96

Kaifeng Communication: The Luotong Highway, constructed by the Department of Construction, has been progressing actively since construction began this spring. The following is the latest information on its status: (1) Luoning Section: From Luoyang to Luoning, the route is 88.0 kilometers long and 7.5 meters wide. The roadbed has been completed, with a total earthwork of 200,000.0 cubic meters. The bridge and culvert projects, except for the Shating River, which used to be a wooden bridge and is now being rebuilt as a stone paved road due to the lack of water at ordinary times, include seventeen brick pier and wooden deck and wooden pier and wooden deck bridges, all of which have been completed, with a total length of 812.0 meters. Eighty brick pier and wooden deck box culverts were also built in July of this year. (2) Wen Pass Section: From the area to Tong Pass, the route is 40.0 kilometers long and 7.5 meters wide. All the earthwork for the roadbed, totaling 114,585.0 cubic meters, has been completed. There are two bridges on the entire road, with a total length of 50.4 meters. One bridge of 18.8 meters has been completed, and 40% of the other one has also been completed. Seven brick pier and surface box culverts and ten cement water pipes have been completed.

Completed (3) Ninglu Section: From Luoning to Lushi, the route is 75.5 kilometers long and 6.5 meters wide. Gōng County Grottoes, Famous Like Yique and Yungang, are Collapsing; Hu Shiqing and Others Form a Preservation Association 97

Kaifeng Communication: The stone carvings of the Gōng County Grottoes in western Henan were created during the Northern Wei Dynasty. Like Yique in Luoyang and Yungang in Datong, they are magnificent spectacles in the world. Their carving techniques are neither entirely based on Chinese traditions nor imitations of Indian relics. They are the result of the gradual integration of the heroic spirit of the Xianbei people, the spirit of Buddhism, and the culture of the Central Plains, resulting in greater ingenuity. Therefore, their exquisite carvings are considered by commentators to be models of Buddhist art in the world, with extremely high value, attracting the covetousness of both Chinese and foreigners. Theft has occurred from time to time. In the past, local gentry Liu Maochan built walls to protect them. Unfortunately, on June 8th of this year, the Luo River overflowed, causing great disaster to the temple. The walls and houses were completely destroyed. As a result, theft has become rampant recently. If measures are not taken to protect them, they will not only be eroded by water but may also be completely lost. Witnessing this situation, Liu came to Kaifeng to discuss protection measures with leading figures from political and academic circles. As a result, he joined Hu Shiqing and others to organize the "Committee for the Preservation of Grottoes and Ancient Relics," located in the Henan Museum. On the 19th, Hu Shiqing, Zhang Zhongfu, and more than 20 others were elected as organizing committee members, and Zhang Zhonglu, Qi Xingyi, Guan Baiyi, Hu Shiqing, Liu Maochan, Liu Xiwu, and Liang Chengqi were elected as standing committee members, with Guan Baiyi as chairman and Xu Yanlu and Bai Zeyuan as secretaries. They are actively proceeding to determine a preservation plan, raise funds, and engage in construction and repair. It is also planned to establish a library and public garden within the temple, so that visitors can appreciate the ancient relics and also enjoy reading and relaxing.

Shandong Province Establishes Regional Farms 98

Provincial government passes general regulations and budget to consolidate economic strength and promote agricultural production and organization

Jinan Communication: The Department of Construction has determined that the agricultural experiment stations that each county had in the past have failed to adequately enhance agricultural production and promotion due to limitations in manpower and financial resources. Therefore, it has decided to discontinue the county experiment stations and concentrate funding to establish regional experiment stations in four zones across the province. These stations will manage agricultural trials and conduct agricultural surveys and promotion within their respective zones. This plan was originally intended to be implemented starting in fiscal year 24, but it has not yet been established due to more complicated preparatory procedures. According to the original plan, the locations for the regional experiment stations were to be Tai'an in the first zone, Huimin in the second zone, Ju County in the third zone, and Laiyang in the fourth zone. Later, Shandong University's College of Agriculture cooperated with the Department of Construction and Department of Education to organize an Agricultural Improvement Association, dividing into research, training, and promotion departments, all located in Jinan. The second zone experiment station will be responsible for promotion. The College of Agriculture's 300+ mu of fields will serve as the experiment station site. Therefore, the location of the first zone experiment station has also been changed to Licheng (i.e., Jinan). Recently, the Department of Construction has completed the general regulations for the organization of the regional experiment stations and the budget for various expenses, which will take effect on September 1st. Department of Construction Director Zhang Honglie presented the organizational regulations and budget for the experiment stations at the provincial government's political affairs meeting today (the 17th). After discussion, it has been passed. The regulations and budget are as follows:

Organizational Regulations: Article 1: In order to increase the efficiency of agricultural trials and agricultural promotion, the Shandong Provincial Department of Construction will temporarily discontinue the county experiment stations and establish regional experiment stations in zones throughout the province. Article 2: Each regional experiment station will be supervised by the Department of Construction and will manage agricultural trials and agricultural surveys and promotion within its zone. The zone divisions are as follows: Zone 1: Licheng, Pingyuan, Linqing, Tangyi, Yanggu, Feicheng, Guan County, Changqing, En County, Qingping, Guan County, Shouzhang, Pingyin, Fan County, Tai'an, Gaotang, Boping, Guantao, Jucheng, Dong'a, Zhangqiu, Xiajin, Renping, Qiu County, Pu County, Ningyang, Qihe, Chengwu, Liaocheng, Xin County, Qufu, Ziyang. Zone 2: Huimin, Linyi, Wudi, Qingcheng, Boxing, Jiyang, Shanghe, Zhanhua, Qidong, Guangrao, Wancheng, Deping, Bin County, Changshan, Linzi, Dezhou, Leling, Putai, Huantai, Ling County, Yangxin, Lijin, Gaoyuan. Zone 3: Ju County, Zou County, Laiwu, Changle, Jiaozhou, Linyi, Sishui, Fushan, Yishui, Rizhao, Tancheng, Fei County, Zichuan, Nuo County, Yi County, Mengyin, Yidu, Anqiu, Teng County, Xintai, Linqu, Gaomi. Zone 4: Laiyang, Pingdu, Qixia, Rongcheng, Jimo, Yexian, Fushan, Haiyang, Zhili County, Zhaoyuan, Muping, Changyi, Huang County, Wendeng, Shouguang, Penglai. Article 3: The first zone experiment station is located in Licheng, the second zone experiment station is located in Huimin, the third zone experiment station is located in Ju County, and the fourth zone experiment station is located in Laiyang. Article 4: The expenses of each regional experiment station will be temporarily funded by consolidating the original funds of the county experiment stations and allocating them by the Department of Construction. After provincial funds are determined and included in the provincial budget, the county funds will still be used by the respective counties for construction and industrial development. Article 5: Each regional experiment station will have one station director, appointed by the Department of Construction from graduates of agricultural colleges with at least two years of agricultural administration experience, or from graduates of agricultural vocational schools with at least three years of agricultural administration or crop trial experience. They will be responsible for all matters of the entire station. Article 6: Each regional experiment station will have one to two technicians, selected by the Department of Construction from graduates of agricultural colleges with at least two years of crop trial experience, or from graduates of agricultural vocational schools with at least two years of crop trial experience. They will be appointed by the director to manage all technical matters. The technicians in the fourth experiment station should be limited to those who specialize in horticulture. Article 7: Each regional experiment station will have one to three assistant technicians, selected by the director from graduates of agricultural colleges or agricultural vocational schools with at least three years of agricultural experience. They will be reported to the Department of Construction for appointment and will be directed by the director to assist in all technical matters. Article 8: Each regional experiment station will have three to five assistants, selected and appointed by the director from graduates of agricultural vocational schools or Class A agricultural schools with at least two years of agricultural experience, and reported to the Department of Construction for record. They will be directed by the director to assist in all technical matters. Article 9: Each regional experiment station will have one to two clerks, selected and appointed by the director and reported to the Department of Construction for record, to handle document, accounting, and general affairs matters. Article 10: Each regional experiment station may use trainees as needed for its operations, with graduates of agricultural schools or high schools as qualified. Article 11: Each regional experiment station may employ employees as needed, depending on the complexity of the affairs. Article 12: Each regional experiment station may establish sub-stations as needed. Article 13: Separate detailed rules will be established for the operation of each regional experiment station. Article 14: These regulations may be amended if there are any matters not covered. Article 15: These regulations will take effect from the date of approval and promulgation.

Security Guard Commits Suicide by Gunshot 101

Hui Shiquan, a resident of Renshi Bridge in the Sixth District, was 28 years old and worked as a shop assistant at the Zhengda Silk and Cloth Store in Nanfangquan Town, earning only six or seven yuan per month. He also served as a security guard in the town's security corps. His parents, wife, and daughter were extremely poor. The day before yesterday, his wife, because her husband had not returned for a year, went to Nanfangquan to find him. Upon seeing each other, they poured out their hearts, and their hearts were broken. At around 3:00 PM in the afternoon, Shiquan, because he had no money and could not afford to send his beloved wife home, had thoughts of ending his life. Therefore, in the bedroom, taking advantage of the unguarded moment, he used a pistol to shoot himself in the chest. With a loud bang, he fell back into a pool of blood, barely breathing. The bullet did not exit. He was rushed to the city and admitted to Puren Hospital for treatment. His life is in great danger.

Local News

Central Trust Bureau Opens This Morning, Central Savings Association to Handle Prize-Linked Savings 106

The Central Trust Bureau is scheduled to officially begin operations today, handling various trust businesses. Chairman Kong of the Bureau has submitted the opening situation to the Executive Yuan of the National Government for record, and has telegraphed various ministries, commissions, and provincial and municipal governments for notification, instructing their respective subordinate agencies that, in the future, for various businesses that should be handled by the Bureau, all agencies should contact and handle them in accordance with the regulations. This morning at 9:00 AM, the Bureau held its opening ceremony. The ceremony was grand. Chairman Kong and Director Zhang both personally attended the meeting. All directors and supervisors were present. The board of directors and supervisors held a joint meeting to discuss business policies. Since the Bureau began preparations, it has been over a year. Various internal procedures have been completed. Since the announcement was made in this city, people from all walks of life have flocked to the Bureau to inquire about business details, and those preparing to entrust business are endless. The establishment of the Central Trust Bureau and the Central Savings Association is due to the new criminal law, which stipulates that any private individuals who intend to operate prize-linked savings for profit or issue lottery tickets without government permission are prohibited. Therefore, the original savings associations had to stop operating. In order to protect the interests of depositors in the old savings associations, the government, after deliberation by the Central Political Conference, specially authorized the Central Trust Bureau to establish the Central Savings Association to manage prize-linked savings in order to transform private into public, encourage the public's savings concept, and it is also heard that the Association, since the government's issuance of lottery tickets is not prohibited in the new criminal law, has changed to drawing prizes monthly, and the treatment of depositors is improved compared with the original savings associations to benefit depositors. The regulations are being drafted. Once approved by the government, they will be announced. At that time, the prize-linked savings of the Sino-French Jia and Yi departments and the China Industrial Bank can be merged and handled, and the methods will also be announced at the same time.

American Ambassador Johnson Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday Morning 107

He is scheduled to depart from Shanghai at 4:00 PM today aboard the Pacific Steamship Company's "General Xiamen" steamer, along with Mr. Okinsky, a League of Nations highway expert returning home after completing his term. According to Mr. Xue, in recent years, highway construction in China has made significant progress, and many provinces have completed highways. However, many construction projects have failed to meet economic conditions and have been wasteful. In view of this, the National Economic Council has specially joined with the Municipal Government to send him to Europe and America to study highway engineering and research economical road construction methods for reference. The study period is scheduled for six months, with two months in the United States and then traveling to various European countries. He is grateful that Mr. Okinsky has agreed to assist him at any time, which will bring much convenience. Mr. Okinsky is of Polish nationality and has been working in China for four years, assisting in the construction of highways in various provinces and achieving considerable results. Now that his term is over, he is returning to his original position in the Ministry of Communications.

Inspection Group to Siam to Depart Mid-Month, Overseas Chinese Telegraph That Siamese Authorities' Attitude Has Improved, Aid to Overseas Chinese in Siam Association Temporarily Suspends Work 112

If the situation is good at that time, the organization of the aid association can be cancelled. Otherwise, it will intensify its work.

Japanese Sinologist Tomita Kensuke Comes to China to Investigate Ming Dynasty Scholars 113

The Japanese "Riyue Xinwen" (Sun and Moon News) reports that the scholars Song Lian and his disciple Fang Zhengxue, during the reign of Emperor Taizu of the Ming Dynasty, had the greatest influence on Japanese culture. Professor Tomita Kensuke of Kochi Prefectural High School has been entrusted by the Department of Cultural Affairs with China to study the relics of Ming Dynasty scholars. He arrived in Shanghai yesterday aboard the "Shanghai Maru". He made the following statement to reporters: "Song Lian was a Ming Dynasty scholar, also known as Jinglian. During the reign of Emperor Taizu of the Ming Dynasty, he formulated rituals and music systems, edited the History of the Yuan Dynasty, and was hailed as the literary master of his time. Envoys from foreign countries all heard of his name. When envoys from Japan, Goryeo, and Annam came to China, they all purchased his literary collections. The Complete Works of Song Xueshi consists of 333 volumes. His posthumous works were supplemented and compiled by later generations. Japanese translations are already available. His disciple Fang Zhengxue inherited his legacy and was also known for his literary talent, becoming famous for a generation. Their theories have greatly influenced Japanese culture. Chinese ancient culture is originally the crown of all nations, but it is regrettable that the Chinese people are fascinated by European and American culture to the detriment of their original culture. I admire Song Lian and Fang Zhengxue very much. Now, in order to collect relics, I have come to China to investigate. The investigation is scheduled to last for one month. I will visit various places and report the results to the Department of Cultural Affairs with China. I will first visit Song Lian's hometown of Jinhua, then Fang Zhengxue's hometown of Ninghai, and then Song's lost territory of Quzhou between Yichang and Chongqing. I will also explore the deeds of Su Dongpo, Tao Yuanming, Bai Letian, and Xu Junqi. Xu Junqi was imprisoned for twenty years and refused to submit to the Qing Dynasty, eventually dying for his integrity."

Hydrographic Office Issues Notice Regarding Sunken Ships Obstructing Waterways, Ship Name "Dexing," Currently Drifting 115

The Naval Hydrographic Office recently discovered a sunken merchant ship in the sea at 118 degrees 56 minutes east longitude and 24 degrees 50 minutes north latitude on the southeast coast. The ship is named "Dexing." The hull of the sunken ship has been destroyed, with half of the ship submerged in the sea. There are no objects inside the ship. It is currently drifting on the sea surface with the wind. It is believed that the accident occurred on the 19th of this month. It is not yet known which company the ship belongs to. Since the sunken ship is obstructing navigation, a notice is issued to inform all ships in this port to check.

Recent Situation of the China Agricultural Cooperative Loan Syndicate, 29 Cooperatives in Shaanxi, Henan, and Hebei Provinces Have Loaned or Plan to Loan More Than 1.7 Million Yuan 117

The China Agricultural Cooperative Loan Syndicate's loan plan for this year will be based on granting production, utilization, and sales loans to cotton production and sales cooperatives in the three regions of Shaanxi, Henan, and Hebei. In the Shaanxi region, the Shanghai Bank is the main operator. 17 production and sales cooperatives have been established, distributed in Chang'an, Weinan, Linzi, Huaxian, Dali, Heshang, and other counties. Production loans of more than 500,000 yuan and utilization loans of more than 40,000 yuan (carried over from last year) have been issued. The sales loans are limited to 750,000 yuan. The cotton of this session will be listed soon, and it is planned to directly transport and sell it to Shanghai, Qingdao, and other places. It is currently being planned in conjunction with the Cotton Production Improvement Institute. In the Henan region, the Bank of Communications is the main operator. There are nine production and sales cooperatives, distributed in Taikang and Zhangde in Henan Province, and Jie County and Yuncheng in Shanxi Province. Production loans have not been issued due to lack of time. Utilization loans of more than 15,000 yuan were issued in the morning. Sales loans are currently planned to be 260,000 yuan. The cotton from each cooperative is planned to be sold to yarn mills nearby. In the Hebei region, the Jincheng Bank is the main operator. There are 13 cooperatives, distributed in Handan and Anci counties. Production loans of more than 26,000 yuan have been issued. It is planned to issue utilization loans of more than 2,000 yuan and sales loans of 60,000 yuan. According to statistics, the various loans that have been issued and are planned to be issued to the 29 cooperatives in the three regions amount to more than 1.7 million yuan.

Ministry of Finance Approves That Documents Bound Into Books Should Be Stamped, Invoice Stub Books Do Not Need to Be Stamped 118

The Ministry of Finance approved the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce's request for instructions on the stamp duty regulations: "Regarding your telegram, since each consignment invoice is stamped individually, the stub book no longer needs to be stamped. As for the internal documents that are used internally and do not generate external rights and obligations, although they can be exempted from stamp duty according to law, if they are bound into books, their nature is the same as the books used in business, and they should be handled in accordance with Article 11 of the Implementation Rules of the Stamp Tax Law, which stipulates that books compiled from loose-leaf pages should still be stamped with stamp duty in accordance with the book example. Receipt, dispatch, leave, and arrival books used by shops or factories do not need to be stamped. However, user name books and work record name books are related to business and should still be stamped in accordance with the book example in Item 11 of the tax rate table. Please be informed of this approval."

Bank of China, Bank of Communications, and Central Bank Stop Paying 23-Year Customs Tax Bonds, Central Bank Notifies Bondholders to Pay Attention 120

The Central Bank was originally designated as the agency for the repayment of principal and interest of the 23rd-year Customs Tax Bonds of the Republic of China. In order to facilitate bondholders, it has specially entrusted the Bank of China and the Bank of Communications in various places to jointly manage the payment. Yesterday, a notice was issued stating, "Article 8 of the 23rd-year Customs Tax Bond Regulations stipulates that the Central Bank is designated as the agency for managing the repayment of principal and interest. In order to facilitate bondholders' access to principal and interest, in addition to the branches and offices of this bank handling the payment, the Bank of China and the Bank of Communications in various places are also entrusted to jointly handle the payment. This is a special announcement."

Shanghai Treasury of the Ministry of Finance to Be Taken Over by the Central Bank First, Request Submitted to Ministry to Send Personnel to Shanghai to Inspect and Accept Immediately 121

The Shanghai Treasury of the Ministry of Finance, designed and drawn by architect Zhuang Jun, was contracted by the Dayuan Construction Factory and construction began on New Year's Day this year. It has now been completed and handed over to the Ministry for acceptance. It is the most fully equipped and largest silver treasury in China.

Treasury Project

The treasury is located in the Central Mint at the end of Gordon Road. The entire length is 140 feet, the height is 23 feet and 3 inches, and the width is 100 feet. The interior of the treasury is divided into two parts, each 54 and a half feet long, 74 feet wide, and 10 feet high. The ground is entirely covered with steel bricks, and the surrounding walls are made of bricks. The walls around the treasury are 24 inches thick, 14 inches inside, using reinforced concrete, and 10 inches outside, using red bricks. The two treasury doors were manufactured by the American firm Shenchang Foreign Firm and are able to prevent theft and fire. Ventilation pipes are installed around the treasury. A corridor is built outside the treasury. The roof is made of reinforced concrete. There are four roof doors, each with an area of 7 feet and a width of 5 feet. The doors are fan-shaped. Steel windows are installed around the outside of the building. The treasury can hold 200 million yuan in national currency.

Accepted by the Ministry

After the completion of the treasury, architect Zhuang Jun reported to the Central Bank, which sent personnel to take over first, and then reported to the Ministry of Finance to send personnel to inspect and accept. The treasury cost approximately 140,000 yuan in national currency. Its complete equipment and large capacity are unique in China. It is named "Shanghai Treasury of the Ministry of Finance of the National Government." In the future, the national currency minted daily by the Central Mint will be stored in the treasury.

Workers of the Zhabei Water and Electricity Company Petitioned the Party and Government Agencies Yesterday, Demanding Revisions to Service Rules 126

According to Dagong News Agency, the commercially operated Zhabei Water and Electricity Company, since taking over the former Zhabei Water and Electricity Company, has been in operation for over a decade. The business has flourished year by year, with more than 400 workers employed in the new and old plants combined. Recently, the factory management, in order to manage workers' work and increase efficiency, specially formulated seventy articles of worker service rules. Among them, the content of Articles 14, 23, 24, 49, and 52 placed many restrictions on workers. Therefore, all the workers reported to the Sixth District Water and Electricity Workers' Union, which, after careful study by the joint meeting of the union's directors and supervisors, deemed it necessary to have a detailed consideration with the factory. They requested a temporary suspension of implementation, which was not agreed to by the factory. Therefore, the union yesterday morning sent representatives Ding Kunshan, Gu Jinfa, Le Lianpin, and Zhao Binxing to petition the party and government agencies. Lu Jingshi, a member of the municipal party headquarters, received them and promised to forward the request to the Social Affairs Bureau to temporarily suspend implementation and instructed the workers to report the articles in the rules that caused difficulties for the workers to the party headquarters for review and handling. The Social Affairs Bureau, represented by Wang Gang of the Third Section, replied that if the workers felt the articles were inappropriate, they could submit a request for revision. The representatives considered the result of the petition satisfactory. At the same time, more than 20 representatives from various departments of the new and old plants, including Ding Alin and Zhang Heshang, visited Deputy Manager Weng Yousan. The manager indicated that he would consult with General Manager Lu Bohong and respond within three days, it is said.

The performance program is divided into five categories: Peking Opera, drama, singing, dancing, and film. Male and female stars from various film companies in the city will perform, and the performances will be exceptionally wonderful. Tickets are priced at one yuan. In addition to being sold at the committee's office on the third floor of 59 Hong Kong Road, they have also been entrusted to major companies and shops for sale. The ticket sales points will be announced in the coming days. The finals for the top ten dance stars elected by the nine major dance halls will be held at 3:00 PM on October 6th at the Great Shanghai Garden Ballroom. The committee will host separate announcements of the final competition rules starting today. Chinese and Western pharmacies in the city have specially made many valuable gifts to be distributed to the dance stars elected in the finals to show encouragement.

Announcement from the Harbor Quarantine Office: Disinfection Required for Import of Used Goods 131

The Harbor Quarantine Administration issued the following announcement yesterday: For the purpose of announcement, all factory bags, used cloth, used cotton wadding, used waste cotton yarn, used clothes, used pillows and bedding, used waste wool, and used paper, etc., imported from foreign countries must be submitted with a disinfection certificate issued by the health official of the country of origin. Those who cannot submit this certificate will have the above-mentioned items quarantined and disinfected before they can be retrieved. All disinfection costs shall be paid by the importing merchant. The above regulations will be implemented three months after the date of this announcement. This is hereby announced.

Radio Registration - Licenses to Be Issued by the Ministry of Communications - Registration Period Expired Yesterday 134

Since the Ministry of Communications ordered the International Telecommunications Bureau to begin registering civilian broadcast radios on August 1st, the two-month deadline expired yesterday. A Datong News Agency reporter has recorded the following:

Deadline Expired

Since the International Telecommunications Bureau issued a notice ordering all broadcast radios, whether tube type, official type, or crystal type, to be registered with the bureau by the end of September, applications from citizens and foreigners who have radios have been very enthusiastic, with more than 68,000 registered. The bureau has reviewed the registration forms and submitted them to the Ministry of Communications for license issuance. Now that the deadline has expired, the bureau's engineering department will soon send inspectors to investigate. If any violations of Article 211 of the regulations are discovered, the households will be fined between five and one hundred yuan in accordance with the provisions of Article 211 of the Telecommunications Regulations.

Notice to Households

The bureau also issued a special notice to citizens to beware of imposters posing as radio inspectors. The original text is as follows: "According to confidential reports, there are currently people impersonating personnel from this bureau to privately inspect broadcast radios in the city, attempting to defraud. This bureau is currently not sending personnel to inspect. In the future, if inspection is necessary, the bureau will issue licenses to the inspectors as credentials and will also publish a notice in the newspaper. For fear that all circles will be deceived, this special notice is issued for general knowledge."

Municipal Public Security Bureau - Tea House Registration Deadline Expired Yesterday - More Than 560 Tea Houses Have Been Registered as Qualified - Licenses of More Than 400 Unqualified Tea Houses to Be Revoked 135

Cai Jingjun, the director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, previously stated that Shanghai is a place where Chinese and foreigners live together, and idlers often use tea houses as places to rest. Those who set up tea houses often engage in illegal activities such as gambling and skimming profits, which has a significant impact on social security. Therefore, starting on the first day of last month, tea house registration was started. All tea houses in the urban area must fill out an application form to apply for registration. After the bureau receives the application form, it will send personnel to conduct an on-site investigation. Those who are deemed qualified will be issued a business license and allowed to register. Those who are slightly unqualified will be ordered to improve. Currently, more than 560 tea houses have applied for registration and have been deemed qualified, and more than 400 have been deemed unqualified. There are still many who have not applied for registration. It is learned that the registration has been set to expire yesterday (30th). Those who have not registered after the deadline or those who are unqualified will have their business licenses revoked by the bureau in conjunction with the Social Affairs Bureau, it is said.

The Fourth Mass Wedding of This City to Be Held Tomorrow; 142 Couples Approved to Participate; Rehearsal Ceremony to Be Held at 2 PM This Afternoon 137

The new lifestyle mass wedding promoted by the Municipal Social Bureau, after being approved by the Municipal Government, has been held for three sessions. Participation has been very enthusiastic, and various parts of the country have followed suit, showing the society's need for this kind of method. The fourth mass wedding ceremony will be held tomorrow, and the rehearsal ceremony will be held this afternoon. 142 couples will participate, setting a record for the highest number of participants in the past. Details are as follows:

Number of Participants

In this session, a total of 146 couples applied for registration and were approved and announced by the Social Bureau after preliminary review. After the announcement, 4 couples were unable to participate due to malfunctions, and the actual number of participants was 142 couples. All marriage participants and officiant seal procedures have been completed. The four couples who did not participate can claim back their registration fees from the accounting section of the Social Bureau after October 1st with their receipts.

Order of Ceremony

The mass wedding ceremony will be held at 3 PM tomorrow afternoon in the Municipal Government Auditorium. The couples should arrive at the Municipal Government before 2:30 PM. The layout of the auditorium will be roughly the same as the previous two sessions. A red carpet will be laid in the center, leading directly to the door. Candles will be lit high in front of the stage, and auspicious banners will be hung on both sides. 142 couples will enter the auditorium to the sound of music, ascending the stone steps from the road in front of the government. The order of the wedding ceremony: (1) The couples stand in solemnity; (2) Bow in the highest respect to the party, national flag, and the portrait of the Premier; (3) The officiant reads the wedding vows; (4) Exchange wedding vows; (5) The officiant awards certificates and souvenirs; (6) The officiant's address; (7) The couples thank the officiant.

For the wedding day, the couples will arrange their own cars. Gaocheng Factory, Bansongwei Section: Completion of Double Tram Tracks; Routes 1 and 4 Tram Service Restored to Original Condition 138

Lu Zhonglin, Chief of the Traffic Section of the South China Electric Company, and Du Ningru, stated that tram lines 1 and 4, running on the Bansongwei Road section of the Gaocheng Factory, have previously used single tracks. Now, in order to facilitate rapid transportation for passengers in the southern city area, the tracks have been rebuilt as double tracks. The latest type of steel rails, sturdy and durable, were specially purchased from Germany. Construction began in early August and has cost a great deal. The project was completely completed yesterday, and from October 1st (today), tram lines 1 and 4 will resume their original routes. This will provide greater convenience for passengers in the southern city area. The company's announcement reads in part: "The tram route of lines 1 and 4, from Wangdao Bridge to Gaocheng Temple, has been rebuilt as a double-track line. It has now been completed. It is hereby announced that from October 1st, all tram lines 1 and 4 will resume their original routes."

(7) Regarding Honorary Gold Medals: Academic organizations in Europe and the United States often award honorary gold medals or medals to those who have made special contributions to construction, in order to encourage academic experts to focus on construction. In small terms, they seek improvements for the country and society, and in large terms, they create happiness for mankind. The articles are perfect, so their countries are becoming richer and stronger, and talents are emerging in large numbers, with all industries prospering. This is not only because they are good at encouragement, but also because they promote it. The association, in view of this, passed seven articles on the method of awarding honorary gold medals at the 14th board meeting. This year, after discussion by Mr. Gu Huichang and others, Mr. Hou Debang presided over the salt-making project of the Tianjin Water Conservancy Salt Industry Company for more than ten years and achieved great results. He also authored the book "Salt Industry," which made a special contribution to the engineering community. The association should give him an honorary gold medal. The board of directors then appointed five experts, Wu Yun Chu, Xu Shanxiang, Ding Sixian, Xu Jiadong, and Xu Mingcai, to review the matter. The review report stated that it met the standards of the association's honorary gold medal method. His book "Salt Industry" is admired by Western industrial experts, promotes specialized learning, and benefits mankind. Mr. Hou has made a special contribution to the engineering community and should be awarded the first honorary gold medal to recognize his labor. This was approved by the 17th board meeting and will be awarded at this year's annual meeting. (8) Regarding the Zhu Mu Scholarship: No one was selected for this fund last year. According to the third article of the solicitation method, the 100 yuan fund from last year should be transferred to this year, and the number of nominees for this year should be increased by one. At the same time, one person may be selected. This year, there were a total of nine essays solicited for the fund. On July 26th, the evaluation committee members selected Lin Tongyan and Wu Huaqing, each receiving a fund of 100 yuan. According to the fourth article of the method, they were awarded prizes of 100 yuan for Cao Ruizhi, 50 yuan for Lu Zhishun, and 30 yuan for Ling Qijun.
