Dafuli, Morphine Factory Case; Police Request Adjournment for Further Questioning; Defendants' Statements All Shift Blame 142

Jin Jiulin, inspector of the French police, Zhang Qianying, detective, and others, cracked down on a private morphine factory at No. 7 Dafuli, Maich Road, the day before yesterday. They arrested five people, including Cai Asheng, Gu Jiahao (mistakenly written as A Quan yesterday), Cai Henian, Zhou Xinlai, and Liu Zhiming, bosses and employees, and confiscated morphine, raw materials, machinery, and other items. They were taken to the police station for investigation. The situation has been reported in yesterday's newspaper. Yesterday, the police sent the five defendants, including Cai, to the First Criminal Court of the Second Special District. Judge Wang Gangxu questioned them. Yao Zhaodi, a lawyer from the Police Department, stated the case, saying that the defendants were arrested for jointly manufacturing opium substitutes and requested an adjournment of two weeks for investigation before filing for interrogation. Then, Detective Zhang Ziying reported the process of solving the case, saying that after obtaining clues, he went to arrest them at 1:30 PM yesterday afternoon. The front and back doors of the factory were tightly closed. Fearing that the defendants would be alarmed and escape, he guarded the front and back doors. Then he climbed in from the drying platform of No. 6 and saw Gu Jiahao and Zhou Xinlai working upstairs, Cai Asheng downstairs, and Cai Henian working in the pavilion. He told them not to move and then went downstairs to open the door and let the detectives in to arrest them. After searching each defendant, he went to No. 3 Sanyu on Lafayette Road based on their confessions and arrested Liu Zhiming. He also presented the confiscated evidence and said that according to the defendants' confessions, Wang Yonghe, who lived at No. 5 Yongyu Li, jointly opened the factory. When he went to arrest Wang, Wang had already escaped. Cai Asheng (36 years old, from Hedong, living at No. 7 Dafuli, Maiqi Road) confessed that Wang Yonghe had gathered me to rent this house for a month. I paid 60 yuan. Wang's capital has not yet been raised. He comes once a day, mixes the ingredients, but hasn't started making anything. I don't know what he is doing. Gu Ahao (34 years old, from Ningbo, living at the same address) confessed that Wang Yonghe brought him in to cook and be a steward. He only worked for three or four days. Cai Henian (33 years old, from Shanghai, living at the same address) confessed that he is from the same clan as Cai Asheng. Because he had nothing to do, he lived at Asheng's place. Asheng scolded him to go upstairs to help with odd jobs. Wang Yonghe said he was making Ajinomoto and promised him 10 yuan a month, but only paid him 5 yuan. Zhou Xinlai (36 years old, from Ningbo, living at No. 12 Yuqing Gongfang, Bayer Road) confessed that Cai Asheng asked him to be a partner, saying he was making Ajinomoto, and the salary was not set. He would share the dividends in the future after making money. Liu Zhiming (35 years old, from Ningbo, living at No. 7 Sanyu Li, Lafayette Road) confessed that he had no shares and was friends with Wang Yonghe. He met Wang on the road yesterday, and Wang gave him two bottles of medicine and asked him to temporarily keep them at his home. Wang left immediately, and he did not know what the medicine was for. The court verified the confessions and decided to postpone the hearing to the morning of October 15th. The defendants were returned to custody.

Child Custody Case; Doctor to Appraise; Zhang Tiaomei and Lin Xie's Confessions Each Hold Their Ground; The Son in Dispute Surrendered Yesterday to Describe Everything 143

Zhang Tiaomei, the Chinese manager of Yufeng Foreign Company on Jiangxi Road, previously hired lawyer Ling Qihong to accuse the woman Li Chuanhong of illegally occupying his adopted son Yixian and disrupting the family in the First Special Court. The Special Court has summoned them twice, but the defendant has not appeared. A new hearing date was set. The situation has been reported in this newspaper. At 2:30 PM yesterday afternoon, the date for the continued hearing of this case arrived. Because Zhang's accused is Lin Baoyi's wife, Lin's wife Xie had to surrender to respond to the lawsuit. First, lawyers Di Bingjian and Zhang Tong filed a complaint, stating that Lin Xie's original home was in Nanjing. At the age of 18, she was arranged by her parents to meet Lin Baoyi (former naval commander), and they began living together. At that time, Lin Baoyi was working for the Tongji Training Fleet, and the original wife, Li, was still alive. They lived together for ten years, and after Li's death, the wedding was held. They then moved to Shanghai, where she met the plaintiff's sister-in-law, Mrs. Wang, and they became sisters beyond blood. Zhang Tiaomei, the plaintiff, had no occupation, so they rarely interacted. Whenever her sister-in-law saw the defendant, she repeatedly borrowed money. After her sister-in-law died in 1931, she repeatedly came to borrow money. The defendant repeatedly told her servants to sternly refuse, avoiding a grudge. She did not hesitate to think hard and fabricate accusations as a basis for extortion. Moreover, Lin Jisen, the defendant's son, named Zhao Cong, has neither the name Yixian nor Jisheng. He is indeed the biological son of her husband, Lin Baoyi. In 1917, her husband advocated protecting the constitution and went to Guangdong to serve as naval commander. To prevent arrest by the Beijing government, the whole family moved to Guangdong. At that time, Jisen was only two years old, and there are photos from the time in Guangdong to prove it. After the affair was over, the family returned to Shanghai. Jisen attended the Chinese and Western Girls' School and St. John's Youth Middle School, and there are diplomas and school registers to prove it. The defendant's daughter, named Wan, married Zhu Yuan of Baoshan. There are definite facts to prove this. It is definitely not something the plaintiff can force with empty words. Therefore, in addition to requesting the dismissal of the self-lawsuit and declaring the defendant innocent, the plaintiff should be punished for false accusations and public defamation under Articles 169 and 310 of the Criminal Law. Yesterday afternoon, Lin Xie surrendered through a lawyer. She claimed to be from Nanjing, 56 years old, and living at No. 74 Tongfu Road. At the age of 18, she married Lin Baoyi as a concubine. At the age of 25, Lin's first wife died. At the age of 28, he made me his legitimate wife. I had one son and one daughter. The son's name is Zhao Cong, nicknamed Jisen, now 20 years old. The daughter's name is Wanjun, now 38 years old. At the age of 28, she married Zhu Yuan as his second wife and had two daughters and one son. The son died, and the two daughters are now ten and four years old and are both healthy. I did not know the plaintiff. Because I and her sister-in-law, Zhang Wang, became sworn sisters and had a very close relationship, we often visited each other, so I met the plaintiff. At that time, the plaintiff repeatedly borrowed money. Her sister-in-law cried to me, and I mediated, inevitably causing a grudge with the plaintiff, so she fabricated false accusations. Then, the plaintiff Zhang Tiaomei claimed that the person she was accusing was the defendant who had appeared in court. She accused her of illegally occupying her adopted son and requested permission to take him back. Then, Lin Zhaocong claimed to be 20 years old, nicknamed Jisen, and that he was the defendant's biological son. He also stated that he had attended school over the years and that Lin Jisen had appeared in court. The plaintiff Tiaomei then claimed that this child was her adopted son and could call witnesses to testify. The defendant Lin Xie insisted that Jisen was her biological son and requested a medical examination. Judge Wu Zehan verified the confessions and decided to postpone the hearing to the afternoon of October 12th, pending a medical examination.

Film Actress's Husband Is an Expert Pickpocket; Able to Steal Eight Wallets in One Minute; Sentenced to One Year Imprisonment After Arrest 144

Ji Jinsheng from Suzhou, nicknamed "Pijing Xiao A Mao" (Naughty Little Mao), made a living by pickpocketing. His technique was very sophisticated, and he could steal as many as eight wallets in one minute. Therefore, general thieves regarded him as their leader. Ji's wife, Cheng Wenjun (also known as Wang Wenjun, from Nanjing, a film actress for the Diantong Film Company), lived with him at No. 29 Maho Road. Ji had been arrested and sentenced by the court more than seven times and was released from prison on March 4th of this year. Ji did not repent and continued his career without capital. On the 22nd of this month, Ji used his old tricks again at a tram stop at the intersection of Nanjing Road and Zhejiang Road, stealing a wallet from Huang Zesheng, director of the insurance department of Sincere Company. While passing the entrance of the Hentley Watch Company on Nanjing Road, he was spotted by Chinese detectives Wang Jiaju and Pang Yutang of the Old Gate Police Station. They went forward to arrest him, and Ji threw the wallet on the ground and tried to escape. The detectives caught the thief and took him back to the police station. Ji then confessed that on the 19th of this month, at the same location, he stole a wallet from Chai Jiangshan, containing 35 yuan and 7 jiao. Yesterday morning, Judge Feng Shide of the First Criminal Court of the Special District interrogated him. The police lawyer Wang Yaotang stated the case, prosecuting him for repeated theft under Article 321, paragraph 4 of the Criminal Law, and claimed that the defendant had confessed at the police station that on September 11th, his wife, Cheng Wenjun, introduced him to Diantong Company as an actor to film in Hangzhou, and that he returned to Shanghai on the 17th. He met several accomplices at the Maurice Market and discussed theft in room 347 of the Oriental Hotel on Xizang Road. His confession was completely consistent with the facts and should be severely punished. Ji tried to deny everything, saying he was being framed. After Judge Feng's questioning, Ji Jinsheng was sentenced to one year imprisonment for repeated theft.

Confirmed by Maritime Surveillance Map: Old Kangwang City Exists Northwest of Jinshan; Wei Juxian Makes New Discoveries from Ancient Texts; This Matter Attracts Attention from Central and Local Authorities 147

Following the discovery of the "Old Kangwang City" in Jinshan, archaeologist Mr. Wei Juxian has conducted detailed research using the book "Maritime Surveillance Map," confirming its consistency with legends. A reporter from this newspaper visited Mr. Wei yesterday to inquire about the details. According to him, the pottery discovered in Jinshan previously is related to the stone tools he found at Qixia Mountain and the descendants of Shao Kang of the Yue kingdom. He once personally visited the discovery site for investigation, recognizing that the pottery fragments were washed up by seawater from the beach. The section affected by the seawater extends for several miles. They are not items found on private land, and permission should be formally requested before excavation. Local sources also state that there are many such pottery fragments in Jinshan (not Jinshanwei). Legend has it that there is an ancient city under the mountain, visible when the water is shallow. Later, he consulted the "Maritime Surveillance Map," which depicts Jinshan connected to the mainland, with the Old Kangwang City located northwest of Jinshan, confirming these claims and aligning with local legends. Regarding the value of the Jinshan relics and their relationship with Shanghai, Jinshan is a hundred miles from Shanghai. Several similar pieces have been found west of Fanwang Ferry and in Zhenru, exhibiting identical patterns. This indicates that ancient Shanghai culture is not as recent as generally speculated. He also stated that the discovery of the "Old Kangwang City" in Jinshan is of significant value due to its deep historical and cultural connections with the South. Currently, the central antiquities preservation authorities and local officials in Jinshan County are paying special attention to this matter, ensuring that no private individuals monopolize or secretly excavate the site. Archaeological experts will be dispatched to conduct systematic investigation and excavation work.

Page 16

Murder of Wife in Great World Case: Appeal Rejected 148

Zhao Jishan, 32 years old, a traditional Chinese medicine practitioner from Zhenjiang residing at No. 71, Xinkangli, Kang Nao Tuo Road, Public Concession, and practicing at Guangyi Hospital on Roberts Road, favored his concubine Zhong Zhen's brother and disliked his wife Zhao Leng (34 years old). On the afternoon of July 3rd this year, he lured Leng to the rooftop platform of the four-story building of the amusement park. Near the railing along the corridor on the side of Ai Duo Ya Road facing the Gong Wu Stage, he picked her up, intending to throw her down to kill her. Fortunately, in the critical moment, she clung to the railing and cried for help. The tea server Zhu Jinfu from Suzhou rushed to rescue her and sent her husband to the accounting office. Zhao was arrested and sent to the police station, and the Public Security Bureau prosecuted him for attempted murder in the Special No. 2 Court. Judge Li Changnian conducted repeated trials and ultimately sentenced Zhao Jishan to five years of imprisonment for attempted murder. Zhao, dissatisfied with the verdict, filed an appeal with the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court, presenting cunning arguments to evade responsibility. These details have been reported in this newspaper. The High Court's Third Branch conducted repeated trials and concluded that the appellant Zhao Jishan did indeed attempt to harm his wife and could not evade responsibility. The debate was declared closed, and yesterday morning, Sun Honglin, the acting presiding judge of the Third Branch, ordered Zhao Jishan to appear in the Third Criminal Court and announced the rejection of the appeal. After the judgment, Zhao was returned to the detention center.

Yong'an Silver Company Case: Shen Zufu and Others Not Guilty; Yesterday Was the Third Verdict 149

Shen Zufu, who served as the manager of the Yong'an Silver Company for one day after its reopening, and Dai Kechang, who served as the manager of the Xiafei Road branch of the company for nine days, were jointly accused of embezzlement and fraud by dozens of depositors in the First Special District Court, along with several directors of the company. Initially, they all failed to appear in court. Recently, due to the court's strict enforcement, knowing that avoidance was futile, they complied and surrendered. Judge Xiao concluded the investigation and ordered Shen to post a 3,000 yuan bond and Dai to await a reviewed judgment, as reported in this newspaper. Yesterday afternoon was the date for the verdict. Neither Shen nor Dai reported to the court. Judge Xiao then opened the court and announced the verdict: Shen Zufu and Dai Kechang were both found not guilty. Deng Jinghuan and the other thirteen people whose whereabouts are unknown have had their trials suspended. The company collapsed again, and creditors sued its directors and general managers to recover their debts. Over half a year has passed, but the court has been unable to proceed with the entire case because most of the defendants have avoided appearing in court. Therefore, the court has adopted a method of trying each defendant separately, judging the part of the case related to each defendant who appears in court so that those who appear in court are not delayed by those who refuse to appear. Yesterday was the third verdict. The first person acquitted was Luo Huafang. The second verdict found Lin Kanghou and Ou Jiancheng guilty. Now only Deng Jinghuan and the other thirteen remain, and their appearance in court is unlikely.

Fang Aying Sues Zhang Wubo: Confirmation of Parentage Case; Reconciliation Attempt Failed; Trial Concluded Yesterday, Awaiting Judgment 150

Zhang Wubo, nearly fifty years old, who works at Yongtaichang Store in Taihefang, Fuzhou Road, seduced Fang Aying, a young woman from Dinghai, and rented a house to live together, eventually having a son named Zhimin. While Zhimin was still in swaddling clothes, Zhang suddenly had the idea of abandoning them, falsely claiming that he was going to Japan for business. He disappeared without a trace. Aying endured hardship to raise her son. Until two years ago, she accidentally encountered Zhang on the street. Thinking he had returned from abroad, she told her then eight-year-old son to call him "Grandpa." Unexpectedly, Zhang not only treated his son as a stranger but also glared at Aying as if he did not know her and walked away. Aying realized she had been abandoned. She thought that her relationship with Zhang was illegitimate and difficult to argue. However, she believed that Zhang, as the father of Zhimin, should be responsible for his upbringing. Therefore, in her capacity as the legal guardian of Zhimin, she filed a lawsuit against him, seeking confirmation of parentage. However, she lost in both the first and second trials. Unwilling to give up, she hired lawyer Chen Zhen to appeal to the Supreme Court, which overturned the previous judgments and sent the case back to the Second Branch of the High Court for retrial. These details have been reported previously. Now, the Second Branch of the High Court has, based on the Supreme Court's instructions, repeatedly opened trials, summoned witnesses, conducted thorough investigations, and sent Zhang Wubo and his young son Zhang Zhimin to the Zhenru Forensic Institute to test their blood for reference. Fang Aying had previously testified in court that Zhang Wubo had contracted syphilis. This kind of hidden illness cannot be known unless one shares the same bed. The examination by the institute also confirmed that Zhang had indeed contracted this type of venereal disease. Yesterday afternoon, Chief Judge Li of the Second Branch of the High Court continued the collegiate panel trial, summoning both parties for further questioning. Lawyer Chen Zhen, representing the appellant, stated that the appellee had attempted reconciliation, offering the appellant 300 yuan for living expenses, but the appellant refused because the amount was too small. Reconciliation failed. If Zhang had not cohabited with Fang and had a child, why would he be willing to make such a sacrifice? This is sufficient to prove their past relationship. Zhang also hired lawyer Xiong to defend him. After the arguments from both sides were concluded, the court adjourned and announced that the verdict would be delivered at a later date.

For temporary vendors, please declare on their behalf that they are also operating within the market and can only accommodate ten vendors. We have scheduled a meeting for all registered vendors at 2:00 PM on September 30th to discuss and decide whether to participate permanently, and we will reply accordingly. If you do not participate, the market fees and advertising fees already paid will be refunded as per the receipts." Bank of China Inspection Report 163

The 91st inspection report of the Shanghai Bank of China Issuance Reserve Inspection Committee states: "According to the regulations, this committee inspected the issuance and exchange coupon reserve treasury used by the Shanghai Bank of China and its branches. On September 29, 1935, Xu Kan, Director of the Monetary Department of the Ministry of Finance, Shi Yansong, Pei Yunqing, representatives of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, Song Ziliang, Qu Jigang, representatives of the Shanghai Banking Association, Tu Huai 　, Qian Yuansheng, representatives of the Shanghai Qianye Association, Zhu　 Sheng, Wang Bingcheng, representatives of each bank, and Zhou Hailiang, Wu Baoyu, representatives of the directors and supervisors of this bank, 会计师式梓　, conducted the 91st inspection at the bank. The results of the inspection are listed as follows: The total amount of exchange coupon issued is 114,531,289 yuan, including 81,718,695 yuan issued by this bank, 19,892,599 yuan used by the branches, and 12,919,995 yuan used by each bank. The total amount of exchange coupon reserves is 114,531,289 yuan, including 73,551,312.5 yuan in cash reserves and 40,979,976.5 yuan in guarantee reserves. The cash reserves accounted for 60% and the guarantee reserves accounted for 40%, which were checked correctly. This is a formal report. September 29, 1935."

Research on the Business Overview of Important Chinese Banks in 1934 164

The Economic Research Office of the Bank of China, recognizing the lack of complete and systematic statistics on China's banking industry, compiled a book titled "Research on the Business Overview of Important Chinese Banks in the Most Recent Decade" in 1933. Since then, two sequels for the years 1932 and 1933 have been published. This book is based entirely on numerical statistics and aims to connect year by year. The sequels each have brief records of the business overview of the banks in the previous decade and each has its own independent value. The economics and banking sectors have found this edition to be a convenient reference for research. The sequel for 1934 has also been published under the title "Research on the Business Overview of Important Chinese Banks in 1934." We have received a complimentary copy and would like to express our thanks and introduce it.

The trial of Wang Fan was postponed for a special hearing and she was returned to custody. The court approved the request and adjourned the joint trial to October 8th. It is reported that the police station recently apprehended another important criminal in Jiangbei, who will be brought to Shanghai soon. In addition, the General Investigation Department previously arrested five suspects in this case, Huang Huaizhen, Xie Doulin, Wang Ruqing, Yu Guanfa, and Li Dejin, and confiscated 69 yuan in silver dollars. They were sent to the First Criminal Tribunal of the First Special District Court for temporary detention and detailed investigation. Yesterday morning, Presiding Judge Feng Shide continued the trial. Wu Yaotang, the lawyer of the police station, stated that after investigation, it was found that the defendants were not involved in the case and requested the withdrawal of the detention. Judge Feng ordered the police station not to prosecute and to release them immediately. The 69 yuan in silver dollars were deposited in the treasury.

The Current National Games: A Total of 38 Units Have Registered, with a Total of 2,668 Male and Female Staff and Athletes Participating. Jiang Xiangqing Resigns from the Judging Committee, Chen Mengyu Succeeds Him. An Entertainment Committee is Organized, Inviting Mei Lanfang to Participate in the Performance 172

The Sixth National Games is scheduled to be held in Shanghai on the 10th of this month. A total of 38 units are participating in this session. Only Gansu, Ningxia, and Honolulu have not yet registered. There are a total of 2,668 male and female athletes and staff. The Guangxi team has already arrived in Shanghai and was the first to register with the organizing committee. The National Games Organizing Committee also held its 12th Standing Committee meeting the day before yesterday to discuss various ongoing matters. The details are as follows:

Standing Committee Meeting Situation

The 12th Standing Committee meeting was held on the 28th at 10:00 AM. The attendees were Gengsheng, Wang Shijie (represented by Hao), Lei Zhen (represented by Hao), Chu Minyi, Shen Siliang, Cai Jingjun (represented by Wang Dadeng), Cai Zengmou (represented by Hu Guisheng), Ma Chonggan, Shao Ruhuo, Xu Zhiyi, Wu Bangwei, Jiang Xiangqing, Zhang Tingrong, and Dong Dayou. Wu Tiecheng was the chairman, and Wang Daxu was the recorder. After the formalities, (1) the preparatory director reported: (A) In addition to the entertainment during the evening of the Games, fireworks should also be set off to add to the excitement. (B) Mei Lanfang should be invited to join the entertainment performance and a Entertainment Committee should be organized, appointing Li Dachao, Chen Xiangtao, Chu Minyi, Wang Xiaolai, Du Yuesheng, Jiang Xiangqing, Lu Shoulian, He Tingran, and Zhou Jianyun as members, and designating Li Dachao as the chairman. (2) The Secretary-General reported: (A) Preferential group tickets are limited to student groups only. Other statutory groups in the city and various agencies affiliated with the municipal government may be given tickets at the discretion of the organizing committee, with a maximum of ten tickets per agency. (B) The method of selling beverages inside the venue has been drafted in conjunction with Deputy Director Pan and should be announced immediately. (C) Whether the swimming competition order should be arranged in the evening should be determined according to the temperature of the day. (3) Deputy Secretary-General Wu Bangwei reported: (A) Among the units participating in the Games, except for Gansu, Ningxia, and Honolulu, 38 units have registered. (B) The corrected table of championship types and the total order of the number of participants has been revised and should be announced again.

Seven Important Cases Resolved

Matters for discussion: (1) Deputy Secretary-General Jiang Xiangqing requested to resign from the Judging Committee member position due to being the head of the Referee Section and having heavy responsibilities. The resolution was approved. Chen Mengyu was appointed as a member of the Judging Committee. In addition to issuing the letter of appointment, it will be submitted for retroactive recognition at the second plenary meeting of the Preparatory Committee. (2) The draft method for issuing visiting tickets for school groups was approved and a letter was sent to the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education. (3) The draft for appointing honorary advisors to the Games was resolved to draft a list immediately and submit it to the preparatory director for approval, issue letters of appointment first, and then submit it to the next meeting for retroactive recognition. (4) The Nanjing Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs sent a letter reporting that the number of staff members of the delegation exceeded the original quota set by the organizing committee. It was resolved to proceed according to the original regulations and no increase would be allowed. (5) The Shanghai Table Tennis Federation requested that the date of the table tennis performance be scheduled and announced, and that the leader and athletes' badges be issued to the supporting staff of each unit. It was resolved that the table tennis performance date would be set for the afternoon of October 16th. The organizing committee will provide 70 tickets for that day to allow entry to the performance. The association should provide its own badges and all necessary equipment for the performance. The venue layout should be discussed with the venue equipment section of the organizing committee in advance. (6) The referees for the Games have been appointed. Should additional referees be appointed during the Games period? It was resolved that no additional referees should be appointed on a temporary basis. (7) The regulations for the registration of journalists at the Games stipulate that a 2.5-inch photo of the person should be submitted, which has caused difficulties. It was proposed to amend it so that if a photo is not submitted, the person can sign the document in their own handwriting to take responsibility. The resolution was passed and handed over to the publicity team to implement.

Two Methods Approved

The method of selling beverages inside the venue of the Sixth National Games: (1) The number of soft drink vendors inside the venue is limited to 70. (2) 40 vendors will be assigned by the Central Department Store and the Municipal Government Cooperative, and the remaining 30 will be registered and assigned by the organizing committee to various soft drink stores (up to three people per store). (3) Vendors must wear white long gowns, with the store's logo on the left chest. (4) Vendors must pay a fee of _ yuan per person per day to enter the venue. The method for issuing visiting tickets for school groups for the Sixth National Games: (1) Schools in Shanghai purchasing group tickets must first register in writing with the Municipal Bureau of Education and be assigned a date. Schools from other regions must contact the General Affairs Section of the organizing committee directly in advance to purchase tickets. (3) Group tickets must be purchased from the General Affairs Section of the organizing committee one day in advance according to the assigned date. (4) Students entering the venue with group tickets must wear uniforms and be led by teachers and staff and enter the venue at the same time. (5) Group tickets are valid for the athletics field.

Yang Xiuqiong and Others Arrive in Shanghai, Scheduled to Perform at the Municipal Government's New Pool Tonight, Jian Jinglun Hosted a Banquet for the Athletes Last Night 174

The Hong Kong male and female swimming athletes, including the mermaid Yang Xiuqiong, participating in this National Games, a group of thirteen people led by Yang's father, Zhu Nan, arrived in Shanghai on the President Jefferson at 12:00 noon yesterday. Grand Arrival in Shanghai

Yesterday afternoon, the Hong Kong National Games male and female swimming athletes who arrived included team leader and consultant Yang Zhunan, manager Yang Long Huiming, female team leader Yang Xiuqiong, team members Yang Xiuzhen, Qu Enzhao, Sha Huiying, Chen Fengqing, male team leader Chen Zhenxing, Li Luomin, team members Fang Zongyu, Zeng Hefu, Huang Xihan, and Chen Qiqian, a total of thirteen people. They presented flowers to　, and the audience swarmed forward, surrounding Yang and his party. They then boarded cars and drove directly to the New Asia Hotel to rest.

Xiuqiong's Speech

Yang, tired from the long journey, only met with reporters after resting. Yang does not speak Mandarin, so Director Jian Jinglun of the Municipal Overseas Chinese Affairs Bureau translated for her, answering questions from reporters. The main points are summarized as follows: (1) Regarding the issue of her marriage, she is still in school and it is too early to talk about it. The reports in the newspapers are all jokes made by friends. (2) Her swimming achievements have been　recorded in various newspapers and are difficult to recall at present, so she cannot answer them one by one. (3) The rumor that she will give up swimming in the future is also a misrepresentation. She is currently actively training to seek further development. (4) She is currently studying in the second year of high school at St. Paul's College in Hong Kong and has asked for leave to come to Shanghai. (5) Mayor Wu previously telegraphed travel expenses, instructing her to come to Shanghai to participate in the open competition held on the 22nd. His kindness is appreciated, but she had already replied by telegram and could not fulfill the request due to team actions, disappointing the mayor. She then went to the seventh-floor garden at the request of newspaper reporters to take photos.

Thoughts on This Trip

Yang expressed her feelings yesterday, which are as follows: "The National Games that I have been hoping for for a long time has arrived. When I saw the towering building of the Municipal Government on the Huangpu River, my heart started to beat faster. This time I have also met many athletes from all over the country and we are exchanging skills. I feel that the National Games is the driving force behind national sports. I started practicing in October last year to prepare for this National Games, but there has been no special progress. This is very disappointing to those who expect us. I hope that I can continue to train and seek deeper achievements. I am very grateful to those who guide and comment on me. Many people advise me to give up, saying that a person must leave at a certain time to avoid being defeated by others. As far as my personal opinion is concerned, if others can defeat me, that is the progress of the entire swimming world, and I am very much looking forward to the discovery of this phenomenon. When Japan first participated in the World Games, they did not understand the freestyle method and only knew the sidestroke. However, in 1924, they had relay swimming participation, and in 1928, excellent results such as those of Takaishi and Irie appeared. In 1932, they won the world swimming championship.

It can be seen that Japan's swimming progress in twelve years is rapid, and their progress is a mirror for the world stage. If our country can send athletes to participate in the World Games, it will benefit a lot. The National Games is a matter of pride for the people of our country, because there is no country in the world that has such a large-scale event. The National Games in the United States is also a gathering of the East, West, and Central United States. This National Games is held in Shanghai, making foreigners more aware that our country is becoming more united.

Jian's Banquet

All the male and female team members departed from the New Asia at 4:00 PM to try out the pool in the Municipal Pool for practice. At 7:00 PM, they attended a banquet hosted by Jian Jinglun, Director of the Municipal Overseas Chinese Affairs Bureau, at the Rain Garden in Tingwan. Those invited to accompany them were Li Dachao, Jian Qingman, Ye Yaotian, Hu Guigeng (representative of Hu Wenhu), Chen Ziqing, Lao Jingxiu, and Yang Zhunan and his wife, more than ten people in total. They dispersed at around 9:00 PM. Yang's younger brother, Changhua, did not come with them yesterday. According to Yang Xiuzhen, her friend said that Changhua is still in Peizheng Primary School and feared that he would miss his studies, so he did not come with them. Chen Yuhui could not make it due to work and will depart on the 2nd. We are very interested in swimming, so we are practicing every day, etc. Yang and others are scheduled to participate in the first Hong Kong-Shanghai埠 Inter-city Competition at the Municipal Pool at 8:00 PM tonight.

The male and female swimming and track and field athletes from Guangxi participating in the National Games, a group of eighteen people led by team leader Lu Qihua, also arrived on the President Jefferson with Yang Xiuqiong and others yesterday afternoon. The male athletes all wore light gray homespun Western suits, military caps, and a name tag on their chests. Full Team List

Guangxi Team Leader Talks

Lu Qihua, the team leader of the Guangxi team, talked to a 　 reporter, saying that the delegation departed from Nanning on the 20th of this month, arrived in Hong Kong on the 25th, stayed in Hong Kong for three days, and departed from Hong Kong for Shanghai on the 28th. In previous National Games, Guangxi did not participate due to its location in the border region and inconvenient travel. This is the first time they have participated in the 6th National Games. There are not many athletes and the strength is very weak, but the purpose of participation is not to win championships and compete for victory, but to learn and observe in this grand event and use it as a help from other mountains. Furthermore, the National Games should be participated in by all provinces and cities to share in the grand event. The reason why Guangxi traveled so far this time is also to express the spirit of cooperation and unity.

First to Register

After landing, the Guangxi athletes took a special vehicle straight to the stadium in the central district to register with the organizing committee, making them the first unit to register for this session. Moreover, Guangxi had never participated in the previous sessions, and this time they did not hesitate to travel, which is worth commemorating. The team members were all in high spirits. Except for Huang Ruiwen, who participated in the 1,500-meter and 10,000-meter track and field events (Huang's results are close to the National Games record of the previous session), the remaining athletes all participated in swimming, and their results are comparable to those of Guangdong and Hong Kong. According to the province, all the athletes participating in the National Games this time, except for one track and field athlete, are swimmers. In the Nanning Water Sports Games last month, they achieved excellent results in the 400-meter and 1,500-meter events.

Li Huitang Loses to Korasha, Shanghai Wins All Against Hong Kong, The Men's Group of the Inter-City Tournament Ends, Shanghai Women Lead 2 to 1 176

The Shanghai-Hong Kong 　tennis match was held for the third day yesterday, with one group each for the men's second singles and the women's second doubles. Li Huitang won first and then lost. Korasha fought fiercely for five sets before winning. Shanghai then won all against Hong Kong with a score of five to zero. Yesterday, in the women's doubles, Shanghai won two to zero. The performance was not exciting at all. There are still two groups of women's singles today after the morning. Based on the situation, the Shanghai team has a strong chance of winning the women's championship. The details of yesterday's match are as follows:

Li Huitang Loses to Korasha

There were few spectators yesterday. The men's first singles match started at one o'clock. De Fu did not appear and was replaced by Korasha. Li and Korasha's ball skills were　matched, and they were evenly matched. Li Huitang's serve was sharp and his volley was also skillful, but his baseline long shots were not as good as Korasha's. In the first set, Li often used his wit and often used net cuts, making it impossible for Korasha to follow. He took the lead with a score of six to four. In the second set, Li first won one game and then lost four games in a row, making the score four to one, with Korasha taking the lead. Then Li repeatedly seized opportunities to score, winning five games in a row, and ended the second set with a score of six to four. It was expected that he would take the opportunity to defeat Korasha, but in the third set, Li missed many opportunities and was defeated by Korasha with scores of six to two, six to three, and six to three in a row, ending the match with a score of three to two. Korasha won with fierce baseline long shots in the last three sets.

Women's Doubles Performance is Average

In the women's second doubles, Ms. Ge Lifei of the Hong Kong team had average ball skills, and Mrs. Zhao Zhengzhao was also quite weak, while Mrs. Korasha of the Shanghai team not only had sharp serves, but also had commendable long shots and volley nets. Mrs. Tuile did her best, so the strength of the two sides was uneven, forming a one-sided situation. In the first set, Shanghai first scored two games, and after Hong Kong won back the third game, they immediately lost four games in a row. Shanghai took the lead with a score of six to one. In the second set, the Hong Kong team softened all the way, losing more than they gained, and Shanghai won six games in a row, ending the match with a score of two to zero.

Last Two Singles Today

The Shanghai women's team has already taken a two-to-one lead. There are still two groups of the second and first singles today. If Shanghai wins one group, they will win the championship. According to the situation, in the third singles, Mrs. Harris against Ms. Ge Lifei, Shanghai has a good chance of winning. In the first singles, Mrs. Hancock against Mrs. Kaito, there will be a competition. The order is as follows: Mrs. Hancock seven against Mrs. Kai　duo at 2:00 PM, Mrs. Ge Lifei against Mrs. Harris at　3:30 PM.

Educational News

National Language Society Establishes Primary Schools, Results of the National Language Competition's Second Round 181

The National Mandarin Education Promotion Association launched the National Primary School Students' Mandarin Competition in October last year, with the Ministry of Education issuing orders to the education departments and bureaus of various provinces and cities to order students from public and private primary schools across the country to participate. Each province, city, and county education department or bureau first conducted preliminary selections, selecting two entries from each group and sending them directly to the association, where they were divided into groups for judging. The judging was then divided into second-round selections and final selections, to show solemnity. The second-round judging has now been completed, and the competition committee of the association has calculated the scores and selected final-round judges to review them. After the names are determined, awards will be given according to the rules. Little Men (6) (2) 182

— Original by Ms. Louisa May Alcott, translated by Zheng Xiaocang

The wine was in a jar, passed around to each person. All three took a sip, tasting some. However, Ned and Tom really didn't like the bitter stuff. The cigars were even worse, but they didn't dare say so. Each of them took a few puffs until they felt dizzy or choked, and then passed the cigarette to the person next to them. Don, however, quite liked this approach, because he had the opportunity to imitate the lowlifes he used to associate with day and night, as if reliving a dream. He drank wine, smoked, swayed, and pretended to be like those people, and soon he even possessed the spirit of those people. So he lightly uttered cursing words. Tom had been following his example, but at this point suddenly stopped him, saying, "You can't be like that: cursing people to 'die a thousand deaths' and 'fall into hell'! It's vicious!"

"Kill, kill! Just play cards, don't preach; isn't it fun to curse people like this?"

"I'd rather say 'Thunder! Big Softshell Turtle'," Tom said, having created this amusing expletive himself and often using it by himself.

"I only say 'Evil spirit'; it sounds better," Ned added, but he was already quite impressed by Don's unrestrained manner.

Spring and Autumn

Tidbits 183

— (Han)

Wang Hu, who once served as the governor of Jiangsu Province, had a dignified appearance and a humorous nature, and he was also quick-witted. When he followed Feng Huanzhang to live in Taiyuan, there was a man in his forties who accompanied him, and every morning he would pour the chamber pot for Wang. People suspected that he was Wang's servant, but upon inquiring, they learned that he was a former subordinate battalion commander. People secretly discussed it, saying that he should not flatter the official in this way, and the official should not use his subordinates in this way. Wang heard about it and said to the crowd, "Are you surprised that he pours the chamber pot for me? There is a hierarchy between us, but the relationship is that of friends. I also often pour the chamber pot for him." After saying this, he looked back at the man and said, "Is that right?" The man laughed loudly, and the crowd also laughed loudly. The suspicions were cleared up with one sentence.

In Hong Kong, there is a Lee Chi-shen Street, which is the property of the late wealthy businessman Lee Chi-shen. Someone in the neighborhood proposed a couplet: "Lee's own profit harms others, this is poverty and riches. Gods hate and ghosts despise, the street knows, the alley hears." This couplet has the same wonderful effect as a certain student's elegy for Kang Youwei: "A nation is about to perish, there must be... Old but not dead is..."

During the second year of the Republic, Yuan Shikai appointed Xiong Xiling as the Prime Minister of the State Council. Xiong and Zhang Jian, Liang Qichao, and others promoted each other and called it the first-class cabinet. People at the time ridiculed it with a couplet: "Turtle, bastard, egg. Phoenix, first-class." This is because Xiong's籍隶 belonged to the Fenghuang of Hunan.

Chatting About Hunan 184

— Hualing

The popular little tune "Peach Blossom River" has now become an absolutely extinct delicacy, but the impression that "there are many beauties on the Peach Blossom River" is probably deeply imprinted in everyone's mind.

It is said that the Peach Blossom River is in Hunan. I really dare not be dogmatic about whether there are many beauties on the Peach Blossom River, but because Hunan Province is the location of beautiful mountains and rivers, the emergence of men of letters, chivalrous men, and great revolutionary figures is indeed innumerable. Moreover, for modern revolutionary history, Hunan and the people of Hunan occupy a very important position.

However, in addition to Hunan's great relationship to culture, Hunan's mineral resources are also worth mentioning. Antimony ore is Hunan's largest mineral deposit. Hunan's antimony ore is not only the most abundant in China, but also ranks first in the world. Hunan's antimony ore is concentrated in the Xikuangshan and Yiyang areas. Antimony is an indispensable raw material for manufacturing military supplies, so its price was very high during the European War, making a very good deal. Only the output from the Xikuangshan area exceeded 1,300 tons per month.

Hunan's antimony ore accounted for half of the world's antimony production three years before the founding of the Republic of China. Now, thanks to diligent excavation, it accounts for 80% of the world's production. In addition to antimony ore, large amounts of aluminum, zinc, manganese, and other metal ores that occupy a very important position in the chemical industry are also produced.

In terms of agricultural products, rice, cotton, bamboo, wood, hemp, tea, etc. are all very developed. Moreover, tung oil has an amazing production. In the first year of the Republic of China, China's tung oil exports accounted for 17% of the total national exports. In the 18th year of the Republic of China, it increased to 45%. This refers to exports to foreign countries. All of these are white tung oil. The red tung oil produced is mostly transported to Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces.

From here, we can also see an overview of Hunan.

A Widow's Will 185

— Guanting

A friend, Mr. Qu's grandmother, lost her husband in her youth, but she raised three sons and lived to be over eighty years old before she died. At the time of her death, there were more than thirty children and grandchildren.

When she was critically ill, she suddenly took out one hundred copper coins from the Kangxi period of the previous Qing Dynasty, and handed them over to all the descendants and daughters-in-law to pass around and watch, and said: "The most painful thing in life is a young woman's widowhood. You can know the hardships of widowhood by looking at my one hundred large Kangxi coins. Whenever I felt uneasy at night, I would always scatter those one hundred coins on the floor in the room, and then go one by one to touch them up from the darkness until there were no less, so that I was mentally exhausted and easy to fall asleep, and forget everything. This is the only method I have used for decades of hard widowhood. Don't you see that every side of the one hundred Kangxi coins has not been polished by my fingers? Therefore, I deeply know that it is not only an extremely difficult thing for young women to be widows, but also an extremely cruel thing. You should all remember that if there is a young daughter-in-law in my family in the future who unfortunately loses her husband, do not persuade her to be a widow. You must know how much life is. In order to win the vanity of erecting a "Widow Memorial Archway" for my family, it is extremely inappropriate to force others to sacrifice their lifelong happiness..."

Nowadays, the so-called "chastity" issue is no longer valued by people in society, and there are fewer and fewer young widows observing chastity. The facts described in this article were told to me by my friend Mr. Qu in person, and I specifically recorded them to show the pain of widows who were under the old ethics in the past.

The Fragrant Mists of Imperial Incense Records 188

— Original by Princess Der Ling of Qing, translated by Qin Shouou

However, in fact, once autumn arrives, dozens of gardeners who are specially responsible for taking care of chrysanthemums are so busy that they cannot do anything else all day long and still cannot have a moment to spare. For example, watering, fertilizing, transplanting, and covering with straw mats when there is strong sunshine or heavy rain, and taking off the straw mats after the rain and at night to allow them to fully absorb the dew; in addition, there were no insecticide powders invented at that time, so the work of removing insects also took up a lot of time.

There are many kinds of insects that can reproduce on chrysanthemums and carry out destructive work, and among them, a kind of small green insect that is good at drilling into the heart of the flower to wreak havoc is the most terrible. Before the chrysanthemum buds have grown, when the stems only have green leaves, there is no sign of them. When the buds gradually grow and are almost about to bloom, they come to the whole family uninvited, gathering on the stamens, chewing day and night, and often chewing all the flowers on one branch. Therefore, during a certain period of time, the work of catching insects is really extremely tense. More than twenty gardeners are divided into ten groups, two people in each group, one hitting two specially made tin cups, squatting on the ground, waiting for the other to shake the small green insects off each branch, but shaking them off is not reliable, and the heart of the flower must be separated and carefully searched in order to eliminate them all. Therefore, each flower takes six or seven minutes of work. We can imagine; there are more than 3,000 pots of chrysanthemums in the Imperial Garden, how much time will it take to inspect them all? No wonder those gardeners are so busy every day! (429)

Biographical Sketches

Visiting Humor Master Lin Yutang 189

— Zheng Yimei

About half a month ago, I published an article "Mourning Wang Junqing" in "Chun Qiu," mentioning the discovery of the missing "Zhongshan Travelogue" and "The Way to Health" from Shen Sanbai's "Six Records of a Floating Life." This article was seen by Mr. Wen Lían, who is very close to the humor master Lin Yutang. Yutang was in the process of translating "Six Records of a Floating Life" into English for the "Cosmopolitan" magazine, so he told him about this. Upon receiving this news, he was overjoyed and invited me to his residence for a chat.

That day, it was drizzling, and the autumn atmosphere was becoming more intense. I took a public bus to Yidingpan Road, walked past twenty or thirty shop fronts to find the entrance to No. 43A, which was a very secluded path. Both sides were lined with trees of varying heights, where cicadas perched, making continuous chirping sounds. Following the path straight in, turning right to the last house, was Mr. Lin's residence. The European-style building was surrounded by greenery, quietly without a sound. A gatekeeper led me in and I sat in the study. Mr. Li'an said, "Mr. Lin is at the Cultural Society and will be here shortly." I looked around and saw rows of books, half in Chinese and half in English. The Chinese books were mostly poetry and essays, and many were classics and histories that modern youth had rejected as old-fashioned. I asked Mr. Li'an, "What are Mr. Lin's views on old and new literature?" Mr. Li'an said, "Mr. Lin accepts new things while cherishing the old, without any prejudice. However, he is most opposed to Europeanized writing, regarding it as a pest in the literary world." As he said this, Mr. Lin returned, wearing a long white silk gown. He looked to be about forty years old, very sincere and amiable, shaking hands with me and exchanging a few pleasantries. He then led me to a small room where he wrote, which had a horizontal scroll inscribed by Ye Gongchuo that read "A Studio of Things Not Done." The desk was almost piled high with pens, ink, books, letters, and stationery. He pulled out a copy of the "Yan Lai Hong" magazine published by the Youzheng Bookstore and said, "This magazine publishes 'Six Records of a Floating Life' in installments. I wonder if there were any other published editions before this?" I replied, "The 'Six Records of a Floating Life' initially only existed in manuscript form. Wang Junqing discovered it and happily showed it to his friend Huang Moses, who happened to be compiling 'Yan Lai Hong' and published the manuscript. Later, Wang Junqing compiled 'Shuoku' and included it, which further spread its circulation." Mr. Lin then asked, "Where are the missing two records? Is it possible to find them?" I said, "The manuscript was with Junqing. After Junqing's death, I don't know who has preserved it. I will inquire by letter." He said, "Yu Pingbo's punctuated edition of 'Six Records' includes a landscape painting by the author, Shen Sanbai, and marks Shen's tomb at Fushou Mountain in Xikuatang. I would like to take a camera to Suzhou to find Shen's tomb and former residence." I said, "Suzhou has a tomb protection association, so the tomb should be accessible. However, the former residence has undergone many changes. According to Shen's account, he first lived near Canglang Pavilion and later moved to Cangmi Lane. I'm afraid even the elders can't pinpoint the exact location." At this point, the food was ready, and Mr. Lin invited me to dine. Besides Mr. Lin and Mr. Li'an, there were also two young ladies. His wife had gone out shopping. There were many dishes, all Fujianese style, including a large bowl of clear frog soup, which was exceptionally delicious. It was said to be Mr. Lin's favorite. With each dish served, Mr. Lin would ask the servant if any had been saved for his wife, showing the depth of his love for her. Soon, his wife returned. After being introduced by Mr. Lin, she shook hands with me and then rejoined the table. While eating, Mr. Lin was also reading a collection of sacred images. Confucius spoke of the need for both tension and relaxation. He smiled and said, "People say that humor can lead to the downfall of a country. But if one were to worry about the country and its people twenty-four hours a day, wouldn't that person become a madman? Can a madman save the country? The so-called 'tension and relaxation' of the sage is the way to adjust oneself." After the meal, he flipped through "Six Records of a Floating Life" again and said, "There is a person in the book named Hongqian, but some write it as Honggan. I don't know which is correct, as it greatly affects the transliteration." I said, "Although there is no way to verify this, judging from the sound, the word 'qian' is in the even tone and sounds louder, so 'qian' should be preferred." Mr. Lin agreed. He also asked, "Do Hengtang, Nanyuan, Wang's abandoned foundation, Wannian Bridge, and the Dongting Jun Shrine in Cuku Lane still exist? Are there still flower festival customs?" He also talked about the Lion Grove. He said, "I visited it a few years ago and felt that the layout was somewhat vulgar. However, every tree and stone in the Lion Grove was planted and arranged by famous masters, so I dare not criticize it. But after seeing 'Six Records of a Floating Life,' which says, 'Although the Lion Grove is said to be the work of Yunlin, and the stones are exquisite and there are many old trees, its overall layout is like a messy pile of coal, covered with moss and riddled with ant holes, completely lacking the atmosphere of mountains and forests. With my limited understanding, I cannot appreciate its beauty,' Shen Sanbai's words resonate with my own feelings. It is truly admirable." Then Mr. Lin said, "Besides 'Six Records of a Floating Life,' there is also 'You Meng Ying' ('Shadows in a Dream') that can be introduced to the West. I am currently preparing to translate it." I knew that Mr. Lin was very busy as an editor for five publications, so I dared not take up too much of his time. I bid farewell and left. He saw me to the door and earnestly made arrangements for a future meeting.

Xiaoxitian (Little Western Paradise) 190

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 19: The Senior Official Cherishes His Reputation and Has a Knack for Knocking on Doors; The New Lover Leaves Her Flesh and Blood and Has No Way to Visit the Sick

Shi Lian said, "Doesn't the new madam want to go back and see her family? And Brother Duocai won't let her go? Well, then, I'll represent the new madam." Jia Duocai couldn't help but exclaim "Oh my!" and laughed, "How can you represent my new madam? I wouldn't dare, I wouldn't dare!" Yueying, crouching in the corner by the wall, couldn't help but giggle. Shi Lian blushed and couldn't speak for a long time. He rubbed his hands nervously and laughed, "Even if you want to take advantage of me, I wouldn't mind. Who told us to be old friends for so many years? I haven't finished my sentence. What I mean is, since the new madam can't get away, and fortunately his residence isn't far, I can go there on his behalf to see how his grandmother is doing. If she's well? Naturally, I'll come back immediately to give the new madam a message. If she's not well? I might as well represent you in finding a doctor to see her. This is not a joke, this is a serious matter.") Yueying wanted to go back, but Duocai wouldn't let her, so she could only worry. Now that she heard that Li Shilian was willing to go, she stopped crying, nodded slightly to him, as if to salute him, and said, "Mr. Li, you have such a kind heart, you will definitely have good fortune in the future, you will definitely be promoted and become wealthy." Shilian ignored her words and smiled at Duocai. Duocai said, "I have no objections. But you can understand what kind of people they are, they are only thinking about money." When Yueying heard these words, although she didn't dare to say anything, she only lifted her eyelids and stared at Duocai twice. Duocai laughed instead and said, "Now that Mr. Li is willing to be your representative, you can rest assured." Although Yueying couldn't help but smile, when she thought about the kind of life she was living, she immediately suppressed her smile and lowered her head. But even though she lowered her head, the small dimples on her cheeks were so charming that they were captivating. (329)

Commercial News

Finance: The Mobilization Order in Argentina Dampens the Gold Market's Momentum; Major Players Remain Cautious

Yesterday, the gold market's momentum failed to pick up and remained weak. The overall situation was calm, lacking any special developments. Major players mostly took a wait-and-see approach. However, the spot market eased due to news of Argentina's mobilization order. In the early morning, the overseas silver market in both the UK and the US was flat. The forward silver price in Monte Video narrowed by 2.5 to 3 basis points. Exchange rates fluctuated. London spot gold fell by half a penny. Reports indicated that Argentina had issued a general mobilization order, and the international situation was becoming urgent again. People seemed to be moving towards action. Although the off-market pre-market price was called out at 88.89 yuan, it lacked support. For a time, supply exceeded demand, and prices gradually fell, dropping to within 4 yuan. Major players then came to the rescue, managing to pull it up. However, the opening was low. The central bank's official rate was announced, with both the UK and the US flat, and the customs gold unit unchanged. The standard gold price was lowered to 920.5 yuan. After opening, the market was stable, and the exchange rate hardened, gradually declining after rising. Banks propped it up and then stuffed it down, with the market briefly falling. The Hong Kong and Shanghai Banking Corporation's official rate was unchanged. Afterwards, the market was propped up again. Later, Sassoon propped up the pound, and the exchange rate tightened. Buyers were slightly more eager, causing the price to rise, but unfortunately, market sentiment was mediocre. Many people sold at high prices, causing another decline. However, supply and demand balanced. The forecast for Indian silver was a drop of three annas. At noon, the market remained stable. However, it weakened after closing. The after-market opened steadily, with slight improvements. However, due to negative sentiment, major players sold slightly, causing a faster and weaker decline. The first telegram from India indicated that silver had rebounded by two annas. The exchange rate hardened and fell. However, buyers maintained the price, so the exchange rate remained supported despite easing. The situation fluctuated. Later, the second telegram from India showed a small rebound of two annas. This was followed by rumors that the central bank had opened 350 bars, causing more buying and a gradual rise. However, it ultimately closed flat. Public bonds for October began to be redeemed today. Shorts had already redeemed more than 85% yesterday. A record of today's market situation follows.

The morning opened at 884.6 yuan, down 1.8 yuan from last Saturday. Dadecheng, Yongli, Hengyu, and others advanced from 4.4 yuan to Yongshoutiao and then fell to 2.3 yuan. Dadecheng, Chunyuan, Yonghuixiang, and Hengyu continuously purchased strips. The Hong Kong and Shanghai Banking Corporation's official rate was expected to be unchanged. Yongli, Xifeng, Yongda, Dadecheng took advantage of the high price to sell strips, dropping to 5.3 yuan. Hengyu initially advanced and then exited, briefly rising to 2.3 yuan, but still declined. In addition, Fuyu and Dadecheng sold and retreated to 4.8 yuan. Dingkang and Yongli bought strips at the low, slightly maintaining the price. Dadecheng or Fuyu and others came to sell, causing the price to fall to 3.6 yuan. Dadecheng Jinjiang Ding Zhengchang, Tongtaichang took advantage of the low to advance again, rising to 5.1 yuan. Dadecheng Maoyong still sold, causing the price to fall to within 4 yuan. However, Hengyu, Fuxing, Yongtong, Taichang, Yingxiang and others advanced, and the Indian silver forecast was a small three annas, rising to 5 yuan. After this, the situation was mediocre, without any special changes. After fluctuating, the market closed at 884.7 yuan at noon, weakening after closing, falling to within 3 yuan.

The after-market opened at 883.1 yuan. Hengyu and Huixiang advanced from 3 yuan to 4.1 yuan. Yongli, Hengchang, Yonghengyu, Chunyuan, Yong and others sold in succession. The domestic market hardened, falling to 1.2 yuan. Although Fuxing and Yonghuixiang advanced to 2.3 yuan, the first report from Indian silver indicated a rise of two annas. Dadecheng, Hengyu, Huixiang, Yingfeng, and Heng sold strips, causing the price to fall to 1.2 yuan again. Fuxing, Yonghong, Kangyong, Hengyu, Richang, and Dadecheng gradually advanced to 3.8 yuan. Citibank stuffed the pound for November at 4.375. Hengyu, Changda, Shenfeng, Qianchangxiang, and Huixiang all sold, retreating to 1.6 yuan. Oil Market: White Tung Oil Appears Strong but is Weak Inside - Various Production Areas Hasten Shipments - 196

White tung oil has been almost entirely gathered from various production areas by foreign firms. Although the current market is experiencing wild price increases, the quantities are extremely small. Ten or twenty tons is considered a large amount, and even three or five tons are enough to open a trading session. Therefore, although prices are rising daily, it cannot be considered a normal market. Last week, the Hankou market rose to 80 yuan per unit, and has since increased to 84 yuan per unit. However, the higher the price, the greater the fear, as the current situation has reached a peak. If foreign firms relax their grip, prices will plummet. If they fall by half, 40 or 50 yuan would still be considered a high price. Therefore, although the price surge is scorching hot, people are uneasy, feeling that the market is strong on the surface but weak inside. Even considering futures oil, with December delivery having exceeded 60 yuan, recent sales from Wanxian were only around 57 or 58 yuan in Hankou. Foreign firms are not as eager to purchase futures as before, so there is a gradual downward trend. Various production areas are increasing output for November and December, and even more so now. Regardless of the situation in Sichuan, Hunan, and Hubei, it is reported that the output from Guizhou province, exported via Hong Kong, could reach thousands of tons in November and December. All are eager to sell at high prices, which is evident in the attitude of European and American firms.
